-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8c64609ee4ad425792326fb3c774ff29_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8c64609ee4ad425792326fb3c774ff29");'><span id='8c64609ee4ad425792326fb3c774ff29_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1138')">1137-1138年</a>，19-20岁</div><div id='8c64609ee4ad425792326fb3c774ff29' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年10月</a>　赴京应试。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年3月</a>　应试不第，遂绝意科目。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='86e92b06c8e3414b8ef979ac460fe413_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("86e92b06c8e3414b8ef979ac460fe413");'><span id='86e92b06c8e3414b8ef979ac460fe413_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1170')">1165-1170年</a>，47-52岁</div><div id='86e92b06c8e3414b8ef979ac460fe413' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　任临安府通判。上启两浙转运副使姜诜。作品：《临安倅通姜运使庭彦启》<div id='poem_1255490' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255490' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255490?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临安倅通姜运使庭彦启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255490")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255490_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255490'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255490'>随牒宦游，莫觌侯门之邃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255490_comment'></div>效官京邑，乃依使节之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255490_comment'></div>引脰知归，扪心自庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255490_comment'></div>窃以当行阙衣冠之会，敞外台幕府之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255490_comment'></div>奔走官僚，居常左顾而右睨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255490_comment'></div>班宣条教，固可朝令而夕行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255490_comment'></div>斯为依托之尤，更觉欢荣之甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255490_comment'></div>恭惟某官壮猷经世，盛德佐时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255490_comment'></div>利器无前，颖若万金之宝剑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255490_comment'></div>直躬不倚，凛如千尺之乔松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255490_comment'></div>心胸罗星斗之华，舌颊振风雷之厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255490_comment'></div>早由简在，绰著事功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255490_comment'></div>更承流宣化之权，受激浊扬清之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255490_comment'></div>执抚宇之政，遐追表海之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255490_comment'></div>畴转漕之劳，远继凿渠之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255490_comment'></div>声名暴白，治行彰闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255490_comment'></div>河图洛书，密寓云霄之直；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255490_comment'></div>木牛流马，仍居天日之畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255490_comment'></div>既课最之屡书，宜恩章之沓至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255490_comment'></div>持紫荷之橐，入居献纳之司；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255490_comment'></div>趋文石之班，常奉清閒之燕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255490_comment'></div>某伶俜一介，历落半生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255490_comment'></div>世科莫并于英豪，家法或馀于孝谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255490_comment'></div>考贪廉之目，庶有取于寸长；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255490_comment'></div>覈勤惰之科，或兼收于一节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255490_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1255490_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年10月</a>　任临安府通判。为强衍之愚庵作记。作品：《强衍之愚庵记》<div id='poem_1255510' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255510' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255510?labeling=true' target='_blank'>强衍之愚庵记</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道元年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255510")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255510_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255510'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255510'>吴兴郡擅水国之胜，为东南冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255510_comment'></div>背城而南，舟行不再舍，水广而益清，山远而益秀，浮图倚空，邑屋合散，旷泽砥平，引睇百里，仙圣之所游而幽人之所家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255510_comment'></div>余之友有强子衍之乐乎此，乃即先庐之旧而新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255510_comment'></div>藩篱萦回，窗户简素，奇花大树，植立就列，相方视址，不改其故，而幽情野态，如在世外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255510_comment'></div>强子日逍遥乎其间，种蔬于园，题曰「抱瓮」，开轩南荣，名以「照膝」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255510_comment'></div>直居室之后，越回塘，为北渚，筑台其末，以领溪山之奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255510_comment'></div>燕坐堂上，隐几而两忘，引觞而径醉，兀然颓然，万虑俱尽，虽千钟三旌不汝易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255510_comment'></div>而顾谓余曰：「将以愚庵名吾之居」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255510_comment'></div>余且应且疑，曰：「强子以智称，居官所向治办，馀虑之所及，视夫人相什伯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255510_comment'></div>为之长者誉其能，杂然无异辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255510_comment'></div>兹欲以愚自名，得无非其实乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255510_comment'></div>敢请其说」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255510_comment'></div>强子曰：「噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255510_comment'></div>人之所甚乐，莫过乎安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255510_comment'></div>外不为耳目之所惑，内不为思虑之所耗，安乎不可以有加矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255510_comment'></div>虚明寂静，内心不生，外物自远，此得道者所能而无所适而不安者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255510_comment'></div>贫贱富贵形于外，毁誉是非交于前，众人穷日夜、骋智巧以与物竞，而愚者胸中懵无分别，此亦无所适而不安者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255510_comment'></div>得道者，非吾所敢望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255510_comment'></div>以愚求安，吾之志也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255510_comment'></div>余于是喟然而叹曰：强子求息于愚者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255510_comment'></div>万物芸芸，各有所息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255510_comment'></div>日息乎夜，月息乎昼，农息乎冬，行旅息乎夕，而况于为君子者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255510_comment'></div>且强子亦知愚者之乐乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255510_comment'></div>疾雷破山，呼声动天，而不能震瞆者之耳：神鬼变化，大地涌没，而不能骇瞽者之目；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255510_comment'></div>存亡得失，哀乐好恶，相寻于前，而不能入善忘者之舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255510_comment'></div>盖其能动者人也，所不能动者天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255510_comment'></div>静可以制动，恬可以养智，人为尽而天真全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255510_comment'></div>善刀而藏则芒刃不顿，离娄索珠而象罔得之，又安知夫大愚之不为大智也乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255510_comment'></div>强子其知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255510_comment'></div>余与强子相谓内兄弟，其相友也久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255510_comment'></div>忆往见其年甚少时，清夜人寂，焚香默坐，盖有意于静者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255510_comment'></div>长而涉世，知味著之为非，去健羡，绌聪明，而自息于愚，亦其本心然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1255510_comment'></div>昔者洙泗之间，子路之勇，子贡之辩，于道无闻焉，而得其传者，离形去知者也，以鲁称者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1255510_comment'></div>余又以知强子之进乎道者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1255510_comment'></div>异日有得，将为子贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1255510_comment'></div>因书以为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1255510_comment'></div>乾道改元十月日，南丰曾某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1255510_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年11月</a>　任临安府通判。为超宗道人妙用庵作记。作品：《超宗道人妙用庵记》<div id='poem_1255511' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255511' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255511?labeling=true' target='_blank'>超宗道人妙用庵记</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道元年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255511")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255511_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255511'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255511'>超宗先生居妙用庵中，千变万化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255511_comment'></div>四通六辟，或生或杀，或纵或夺，点铁成金，指南作北，横拈倒用，于法自在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255511_comment'></div>如摩尼珠随现五色，如老大悲千手现前，无有间断，无有疲劳，无有穷尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255511_comment'></div>欢喜赞叹，比比皆是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255511_comment'></div>时有无得居士，致问来者：「汝亦识所谓妙用者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255511_comment'></div>先生泊然太虚，无所附着，杳然深渊，不见源底。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255511_comment'></div>如金刚杵，触之者碎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255511_comment'></div>如大火聚，近之者󵭓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255511_comment'></div>彻内彻外，了无一物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255511_comment'></div>石光雷声，满虚空界，不见纵迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255511_comment'></div>如世伎儿，幻出物象，适从何来，可骇可笑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255511_comment'></div>如张空拳，诳吓小儿，啼止张开，元无所有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255511_comment'></div>识此乃为识妙用者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255511_comment'></div>咄哉来者！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255511_comment'></div>先生微露头角，使汝犹得见闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255511_comment'></div>万一收捲波澜，销镕剑戟，坐断要津，塞却唇吻，汝又将于何见先生耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255511_comment'></div>昔有维摩诘者，不披袈裟，不去须发，游行俗间，为诸菩萨、声闻解去法缚，将释迦世尊慈悲救物所立教言，一一扫除，不遗馀力，名报佛恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255511_comment'></div>又将见大见小，见远见近，见净见秽，见圣见凡，一切分别破坏净尽，名度众生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255511_comment'></div>若但以取香积饭，断妙喜界，有大神力，睹维摩诘，未为知音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255511_comment'></div>今者汝复欲以此观先生耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255511_comment'></div>若能于无作用时常相对面，不为幻躯之所隔碍，始知先生终日为而未尝为，终日言而未尝言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255511_comment'></div>妙用纵横，不离当处，开大施门，不虚设矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255511_comment'></div>居士一日谒先生于是庵，谓居士曰：「汝其记此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255511_comment'></div>闻命之次，奋笔直书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255511_comment'></div>虽然，一点一画，个中容受不得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255511_comment'></div>先生终日说法，一毫也说不著，而况引纸濡墨，文彩愈彰，去道益远，读之者须知居士不曾作如是说，庶几免相负累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255511_comment'></div>乾道元年十一月癸酉，无得居士记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1255511_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年3月</a>　任临安府通判。有《直节堂记》<div id='poem_1255512' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255512' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255512?labeling=true' target='_blank'>直节堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道二年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255512")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255512_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255512'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255512'>王子居室之东南，钜竹盈亩，蔚然而青，煜然而泽，颀然而长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255512_comment'></div>身过其下者视为上，行为迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255512_comment'></div>清风爽气回薄襟袖间，如执热而濯、负载而休、倦游而还故乡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255512_comment'></div>然弃于一隅，有斯须之爱，而不可以常也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255512_comment'></div>王子病之，乃即其北为堂四楹，宏敞靓深，以燕以游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255512_comment'></div>向之林立者，一旦森列庭下，因指谓客曰：「草木之可录者众，桃杏李梅之华盛矣，而不足于清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255512_comment'></div>兰芷菹篱之质清矣，而不足于劲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255512_comment'></div>吾所取友，其惟此君乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255512_comment'></div>将以『直节』名吾堂，子其为我记」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255512_comment'></div>客曰：「噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255512_comment'></div>彼之见取于王子者，其必有道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255512_comment'></div>夫求箭者于会稽，制笛者于蕲春，度杖者于邛崃，东南之美并周于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255512_comment'></div>材则材矣，众人利之，而好事者不忍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255512_comment'></div>色涵烟露，声挟风雨，檀栾婵娟，生意媚好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255512_comment'></div>美则美矣，好事者悦之，而非君子之所敬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255512_comment'></div>若夫干霄而上，不待矫揉，遂其天资而无所屈，不为欹形诡状，勾身侧足，以相媚悦，寒暑犹是，荣悴犹是，凛凛乎志气之不可夺也，超超乎其忘荣辱也，其使百世之下，懦夫有立志者欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255512_comment'></div>其折而不挠，近古社稷臣者欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255512_comment'></div>斯王子之所为敬也耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255512_comment'></div>不取其姿而取其意，不取其意而取其德，爱竹一也，独得其远且大者，岂知之极深者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255512_comment'></div>岂王子之所存固然耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255512_comment'></div>始竹之植乎此也，杖履之所不留，觞豆之所不至，翛然冷然，不为无人而改也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255512_comment'></div>今去几席不能寻丈，人意则异矣，而竹犹故也，又见其终身不易其操者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255512_comment'></div>其见取也固宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255512_comment'></div>王子宦游再终星，两为县公，以能见称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255512_comment'></div>抽身于公府，息驾于私室，而粲然辉光，发于草木，又能托物以自励，其志远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255512_comment'></div>凡人之寓兴，多得其近似之者，因是可以观其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255512_comment'></div>吾愿王子勉之，以有成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255512_comment'></div>自今以始，朝于是，夕于是，俯仰乎高标，游息乎清阴，英华膏润，沦人肌骨，将日与之俱化而不自知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255512_comment'></div>其渐人也速，感人也深，王子之善取友也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255512_comment'></div>王子曰：「是吾心也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255512_comment'></div>客曰：「未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255512_comment'></div>岁晚凝冱，万物改色，尝试与子坐于堂上，下有挺然自若、强项风雪中者，举目得之，欣然领会，子其于斯时乎取之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1255512_comment'></div>王子逌然而笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1255512_comment'></div>客因书以为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1255512_comment'></div>乾道丙戌三月既望，南丰曾某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1255512_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年5月</a>　王炎临安知府，上启致贺。作品：《临安倅通王帅启》<div id='poem_1255491' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255491' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255491?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临安倅通王帅启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255491")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255491_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255491'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255491'>备数群司，尝遵泉府之约束；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255491_comment'></div>效官上国，复承大帅之教条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255491_comment'></div>幸会自天，依归有地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255491_comment'></div>恭惟某官学该今古，道贯圣贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255491_comment'></div>气俱备于四时，身独兼于数器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255491_comment'></div>温润而泽，璠玙居清庙之先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255491_comment'></div>廉折以清，琴瑟冠雅歌之首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255491_comment'></div>凛凛神锋之隽，恢恢游刃之优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255491_comment'></div>冰鉴洞然，或指已经于平子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255491_comment'></div>规抚远矣，咸推自有于夷吾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255491_comment'></div>智略屡凑于上前，人物独高于朝右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255491_comment'></div>坐郎官之帐，列宿增辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255491_comment'></div>乘使者之车，二星动色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255491_comment'></div>遂付神京之剧，行跻禁路之严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255491_comment'></div>直道自将，允矣贵强之莫夺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255491_comment'></div>持心不扰，宴然贫弱之举安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255491_comment'></div>褒嘉时出于枫宸，论撰遂居于芸阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255491_comment'></div>总戎一道，已兼二辅之权；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255491_comment'></div>著绩当时，远继三王之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255491_comment'></div>威名暴白，治行彰闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255491_comment'></div>鳞比万家，尽起裤襦之咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255491_comment'></div>日围千里，自稀桴鼓之鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255491_comment'></div>既课最之屡书，宜恩章之沓至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255491_comment'></div>持紫荷之橐，入居献纳之司；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255491_comment'></div>趋文石之班，常奉清閒之燕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255491_comment'></div>某伶俜一介，历落半生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255491_comment'></div>论材宜在于弃捐，持己粗知于谨畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255491_comment'></div>偶叨官使，获备属僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255491_comment'></div>五月报成，已莫效涓埃之助；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255491_comment'></div>四方取法，将与观竹帛之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255491_comment'></div>惟务恭承，庶逃大谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255491_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1255491_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　临安通判任满，有交代新任李迎启。作品：《临安任满通交代李倅彦将启》<div id='poem_1255492' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255492' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255492?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临安任满通交代李倅彦将启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255492")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255492_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255492'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255492'>结绶登朝，久负妨贤之诮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255492_comment'></div>及瓜请代，尚怀先长之惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255492_comment'></div>托厚契于子孙，酬愿言于曩者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255492_comment'></div>恭惟某官身兼众美，材过万夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255492_comment'></div>落落高标，人共推于国器；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255492_comment'></div>恢恢游刃，世咸仰于吏师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255492_comment'></div>迨兹扬历之多，绰有事功之著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255492_comment'></div>宜在要津而行志，尚须烦使以观材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255492_comment'></div>辇毂浩繁，暂倚题舆之重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255492_comment'></div>丝纶清润，寖升持橐之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255492_comment'></div>难留奔逸之踪，姑借扶摇之便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255492_comment'></div>某仰高有素，结好自今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255492_comment'></div>愧在卢前，益觉妄庸之不称；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255492_comment'></div>请从隗始，更欣贤俊之方来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255492_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1255492_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年2月17日</a>　闲居临安。梁克家除签书枢密院事，上启致贺。作品：《贺梁枢密启》<div id='poem_1255472' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255472' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255472?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺梁枢密启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年2月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255472")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255472_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255472'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255472'>伏审宠膺宸綍，进翼元枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255472_comment'></div>仰庙社之奠安，翕官师之鼓舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255472_comment'></div>窃以男子有四方之志，盖间气之所钟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255472_comment'></div>圣人为百世之师，实生民之共仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255472_comment'></div>虽能设教以垂世，岂皆行道而得时，孰若言之于不讳之朝，施之于有为之日？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255472_comment'></div>恭惟盛世，懋建宏规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255472_comment'></div>广数路以招徕，诗书礼乐以造士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255472_comment'></div>选群公而倚用，左右前后皆正人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255472_comment'></div>至于魁一世之英材，荷上天之大任，是为兼美，允属真儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255472_comment'></div>当射策于王庭，已见致君之定论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255472_comment'></div>暨参华于政路，乃酬康世之初心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255472_comment'></div>既首被于言扬，复踵闻于身见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255472_comment'></div>宜风声之四达，致欢喜之一词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255472_comment'></div>恭惟某官觉在民先，任从天降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255472_comment'></div>力干千钧之重，气回万物之春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255472_comment'></div>地负海涵，独禀佐王之学识；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255472_comment'></div>鸾停鹄峙，共观华国之表仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255472_comment'></div>为一时多士之师，立百世懦夫之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255472_comment'></div>起贵名于日月，际盛会于风云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255472_comment'></div>寓禁直于北门，尝受代言之任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255472_comment'></div>列从臣于东省，更高批敕之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255472_comment'></div>方作命之亟颁，知登庸之有日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255472_comment'></div>某伶俜弱植，孤陋寡闻，早失足于世科，偶寄身于吏役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255472_comment'></div>望馀光于阶戺，获瞻山岳之崇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255472_comment'></div>记孤迹于门阑，方赖炉锤之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255472_comment'></div>敢叙欢忻之意，益抒祈向之诚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1255472_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年4月3日</a>　闲居临安。有《棣华堂记》<div id='poem_1255513' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255513' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255513?labeling=true' target='_blank'>棣华堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年4月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255513")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255513_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255513'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255513'>余筑室龟溪之上，长乐林夫子踵至，暇日相从游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255513_comment'></div>一日语余曰：「吾之友有卨君者，居于渝上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255513_comment'></div>其先人以文材被荐扬，以忠节死王事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255513_comment'></div>卨君与季处，伤夫遗体之不可复益矣，则交相砥砺，共甘苦以终其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255513_comment'></div>又于所居之旁，辟地以观游，名其堂曰『棣华』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255513_comment'></div>志可嘉也，子其为彼识之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255513_comment'></div>余逡巡对曰：余虽与卨君未际也，不知其人，视其友，卨君之为端人也必矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255513_comment'></div>敢诵其说，夫子则择之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255513_comment'></div>夫三荆之感足以还离居之心，束箭之譬足以坚忍死之托，况于《棠棣》之诗，《小雅》之所赋，周公之所叹，而孔氏之所取也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255513_comment'></div>命物以托兴，揭名以见志，至矣夫，其用心也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255513_comment'></div>余知夫卨氏伯仲之居是堂也，偶坐俪立以交其驩，徘徊游息以同其志，豆觞弦歌以合其乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255513_comment'></div>至于春草池塘之思，夜床风雨之适，则必相从以相亲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255513_comment'></div>陈之以诗书，观之以图史，设疑问难以穷其所当然，研究曲折以求其所指归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255513_comment'></div>至夫会意也，涣然而信，欢然而喜，则必相资以相成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255513_comment'></div>惟其先人之德善劳烈，忘其身之谋，而徇于国家，以寿夫后之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255513_comment'></div>凡起居饮食之间，可不知其自也邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255513_comment'></div>穆然而深思，悄然而长怀，则必相泣以相命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255513_comment'></div>士生于世，惟出与处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255513_comment'></div>处而在野，则养生治性，睦姻族，接邻里，乡党无间言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255513_comment'></div>出而仕于朝，则蹈义赴节，全其令名，不为先人羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255513_comment'></div>以至为酥为酪之称，得龙得虎之目，则必相勉以相期也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255513_comment'></div>志立而行益成，业广而名益彰，积善在躬，宠荣随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255513_comment'></div>异时高车结驷，并驱于里门，乡人父老聚首而观，合辞而叹，则又相映以相耀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255513_comment'></div>是数者，举类夫棠棣之为华，枝叶之条达，跗萼之固结，相承以相辉者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255513_comment'></div>卨氏之有闻于时，其必自斯堂始矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255513_comment'></div>古者圣贤之进乎德也，凡盘杅几杖皆铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255513_comment'></div>今则接武堂上，仰视栋梁间而大书在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255513_comment'></div>退而求夫每事之必称，则伯仲之好，愈久而愈坚，虽至于数千百年可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255513_comment'></div>是亦进德之微意，而可为卨氏贺者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255513_comment'></div>匪惟卨氏之福也，凡过卨氏之庐，属目于斯，皆将有感焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255513_comment'></div>是又可以为夫人之劝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255513_comment'></div>然则命名之效，岂浅浅也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1255513_comment'></div>若夫栋宇榱题之制，广袤寻丈之数，带以台沼，缭以径术，松竹之所布，花草之错处，登斯堂者，当能赋之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1255513_comment'></div>乾道六年四月三日，南丰曾某记。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1255513'></div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1255513_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
新城街道（新城）

-----title
南京
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='62bb2c00c6f5483abe5c98dbe7c53d6f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("62bb2c00c6f5483abe5c98dbe7c53d6f");'><span id='62bb2c00c6f5483abe5c98dbe7c53d6f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1154')">1145-1154年</a>，27-36岁</div><div id='62bb2c00c6f5483abe5c98dbe7c53d6f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年</a>　上书建康留守晁谦之，希求援引。作品：《上建康晁留守恭道启》<div id='poem_1255484' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255484' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255484?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上建康晁留守恭道启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255484")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255484_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255484'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255484'>光尘在望，高深惊龙虎之奇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255484_comment'></div>文字为容，庶几同禽鸟之贽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255484_comment'></div>既叨与进，敢遂陈情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255484_comment'></div>窃念某志或妄庸，质难强勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255484_comment'></div>早失庭趋之训，谬传家有之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255484_comment'></div>追祖考之绪馀，已隳世业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255484_comment'></div>缘父兄之保任，仅玷官联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255484_comment'></div>甔石倚墙，空空如也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255484_comment'></div>诗书束阁，望望去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255484_comment'></div>穷且益坚，岂遂忘于先志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255484_comment'></div>时哉易失，已深负于初心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255484_comment'></div>何图漂泊之孤踪，乃获览观于乐国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255484_comment'></div>山川四合，设表里于留都；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255484_comment'></div>宫殿千门，待往来之清跸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255484_comment'></div>递歌谣于比屋，肃号令于三军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255484_comment'></div>久怀慕蔺之素心，今副识韩之始愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255484_comment'></div>裹趑趄之足，俄遂及门；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255484_comment'></div>戴忸怩之颜，措焉无地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255484_comment'></div>贤愚相去，何啻九牛之毛？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255484_comment'></div>巨细兼收，岂异一狐之腋？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255484_comment'></div>无能为役，所慕执鞭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255484_comment'></div>恭惟某官孕秀星辰，毓灵河岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255484_comment'></div>富忠言之活国，伟厚德之照人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255484_comment'></div>隐然家声，著在国史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255484_comment'></div>或出或处，无愧古人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255484_comment'></div>有德有言，可传来世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255484_comment'></div>弁髦翼翼，皆一时人物之英；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255484_comment'></div>印组累累，为八朝氏族之冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255484_comment'></div>欲扶昌运，更出伟人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255484_comment'></div>书汉家镇抚之功，膺周室保釐之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255484_comment'></div>旗旄道从，辍禁直于九重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255484_comment'></div>樽俎笑谈，折遐冲于千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1255484_comment'></div>独当一面，坐成夹辅之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1255484_comment'></div>助理万机，行即前疑之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1255484_comment'></div>斯文允赖，多士所归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1255484_comment'></div>某自怜末路之微踪，方借后陈之馀地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1255484_comment'></div>蓄马渤以待用，或庶几焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1255484_comment'></div>割牛心而知名，非敢望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1255484_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1255484_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年</a>　闲居建康。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年</a>　代从兄为伯母苏氏作行状。作品：《代从兄作伯母事述》<div id='poem_1255517' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255517' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255517?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代从兄作伯母事述</a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255517")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255517_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255517'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255517'>某人姓苏氏，眉州眉山人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255517_comment'></div>眉山之苏，族系世出，具在外氏家牒与国史所载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255517_comment'></div>外祖讳某，某官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255517_comment'></div>外祖母某氏，某国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255517_comment'></div>是生某人，于伦次为季。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255517_comment'></div>年十有九，归曾氏，二十有某年而嫠，又二十有某年而卒于子之官舍，时绍兴丁卯七月十有七日也，享年七十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255517_comment'></div>封太宜人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255517_comment'></div>子恪、慥，早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255517_comment'></div>悟，擢进士第，为亳州士曹掾，骂贼死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255517_comment'></div>事闻，诏赠承事郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255517_comment'></div>怡，右朝奉郎，太府丞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255517_comment'></div>恽，右从事郎，常州录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255517_comment'></div>憺，出后叔父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255517_comment'></div>孙熹，右迪功郎，监建康府都税院；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255517_comment'></div>焘、某某未官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255517_comment'></div>孙女三人：长嫁右文林郎张遹，馀在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255517_comment'></div>某人幼而端庄，不见喜愠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255517_comment'></div>外伯父端明公特奇爱之，字以季安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255517_comment'></div>出于儒家，生长见闻，动有法度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255517_comment'></div>至于智识高明，无妒忌之心，盖出天性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255517_comment'></div>元祐初，我祖父曲阜公、外祖父栾城公志同道合，并擢侍从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255517_comment'></div>先人始以胄子拜栾城公于京师，一见而请婚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255517_comment'></div>时公兄弟道德文章为海内宗师，富贵荣光，实甲天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255517_comment'></div>某人入门，循循无骄人色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255517_comment'></div>曲阜公性高严，家人父子之间，未尝以辞色假之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255517_comment'></div>每见，谓能尽妇道，祖母爱之，为诸妇最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255517_comment'></div>曲阜公同气十六人，婚姻皆大家，内外宗党相扳援，常数百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255517_comment'></div>群居俨然，不强笑语以相媚悦，而上承尊属，旁睦娣姒，自敌以下，纳以恩意，内外怀附，交口誉叹，积数十年如一日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255517_comment'></div>先人既遭闵凶，仕虽不遇，必奉太夫人与俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255517_comment'></div>太夫人雅好客，所居室尝择要地，亲宾四来，燕享无虚日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255517_comment'></div>某人几伺颜色，辄能得其指意，太夫人以忘其贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255517_comment'></div>先人无禄早世，素不殖生产，某人痛自约损以字孤，均一之德，能人所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1255517_comment'></div>屡哭所爱子，人不堪其忧，而某人居隐约之中，当忧患之来，泊如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1255517_comment'></div>平生服用俭素，耻事华靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1255517_comment'></div>春秋既高，精力不少衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1255517_comment'></div>閒为子姓道前事，亹亹不休，听者忘其疲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1255517_comment'></div>岁时上寿，华颠象服，宗党敬焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1255517_comment'></div>不幸属疾，犹谆谆家事如平时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1255517_comment'></div>既病，一置不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1255517_comment'></div>有请所欲言者，曰：「吾胸中无遗恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1255517_comment'></div>若死生之变，安之久矣，复何道」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1255517_comment'></div>泊然而逝，曾不怛化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1255517_comment'></div>某荷遗泽，列著定官行朝，仅得三进封号，尚几期颐，以遂乌鸟之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1255517_comment'></div>今已矣，夫创钜痛深，天实为之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1255517_comment'></div>曾氏世家建昌之南丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1255517_comment'></div>曾祖太师鲁国公讳某，祖少师曲阜文昭公讳某，皆即葬旁郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1255517_comment'></div>其墓在润州者，实自祖母兖国夫人强氏始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1255517_comment'></div>而先人有通直郎讳某，窆于丹徒县长山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1255517_comment'></div>其不肖孤既弗克奉先人之绪，违天负神，以底酷罚，乃以某年月日，谨窀穸之奉而合祔焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1255517_comment'></div>已事，乃忍死啜泣而言曰：「生不能显扬光大，以极其养，殁犹当假辞以传后人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1255517_comment'></div>知吾母之详，宜莫如舅氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1255517_comment'></div>且先人之葬既受赐矣，舅氏当不我拒，谨掇其大略以请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1255517_comment'></div>伏惟哀怜而诺之，以宥其遗孤，且以慰先夫人于九原」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1255517_comment'></div>某年月日，孤某述。</div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1255517_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1154')">1148-1154年</a>　闲居建康。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
长兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6b2fd260ad444f749205e0834ea57791_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6b2fd260ad444f749205e0834ea57791");'><span id='6b2fd260ad444f749205e0834ea57791_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1157')">1155-1157年</a>，37-39岁</div><div id='6b2fd260ad444f749205e0834ea57791' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年4月</a>　以世赏得官，初为右宣义郎湖州长兴县丞。作品：《左朝请大夫前知建昌军陆公行状》<div id='poem_1255515' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255515' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255515?labeling=true' target='_blank'>左朝请大夫前知建昌军陆公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255515")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255515_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255515'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255515'>公讳时雍，字尧夫，世为严州淳安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255515_comment'></div>曾大父某，大父某，潜德不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255515_comment'></div>父某，始以公贵赠右朝散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255515_comment'></div>公幼警敏，为婴儿时已不凡，能以指画字问人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255515_comment'></div>七岁知读书，十三能属文，乡先生往往奇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255515_comment'></div>大夫公以告其家人曰：「此子他日大吾门，汝毋忧贫」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255515_comment'></div>年十四，丁外艰，执丧如成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255515_comment'></div>退即夙夜强学，期以起家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255515_comment'></div>三舍法行，公始游乡校，比比居高等，始有闻于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255515_comment'></div>诸生日廪食县官，公自取疏粝，而储其资以归养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255515_comment'></div>既而与贡书，居上庠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255515_comment'></div>阅七年，有诏释褐，赐上舍出身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255515_comment'></div>方腊窃发，太夫人在乡邑，公时未注籍，闻盗，即日驰归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255515_comment'></div>越明年，始以试学官中选，得福州教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255515_comment'></div>秩满，改池州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255515_comment'></div>训导不苟，所至学者归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255515_comment'></div>入为秘书丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255515_comment'></div>在馆二年，求补外以便迎养，得通判湖州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255515_comment'></div>是年，天子祀南郊，泽流诸臣，太夫人年踰八十矣，躬享封号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255515_comment'></div>捧诏拜舞，起入为寿，母子欣欣，闻者歆艳，谓公孝养诚笃，率如其志云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255515_comment'></div>湖州自军兴以来，事出一切差其民之贫富，使入粟县官而予之直，督索同赋租，官私俱病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255515_comment'></div>至是，公请于州，积钱于场，与民为市，未期月而足，民不告困，郡人至今赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255515_comment'></div>其馀去害就利者类如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255515_comment'></div>秩满，求奉祠以养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255515_comment'></div>无几何，太夫人感疾，公忧形于色，昼不饭，夜不寝，以致力乎医药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255515_comment'></div>既遭艰棘，衔哀柴瘠，每恸几绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255515_comment'></div>至负土石封其坟，不茹荤者终丧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255515_comment'></div>乡闾父老交口叹嗟，以诏其子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255515_comment'></div>服除，通判襄阳府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255515_comment'></div>襄阳新免兵革，民未土著，公劝课劳来，抚摩疲瘵，朝廷之德泽无所壅，疲民以故不转徙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255515_comment'></div>签书枢密院事詹公某以使事出疆，会公还朝，因请掌记室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255515_comment'></div>归报，除知建昌军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1255515_comment'></div>虔州戍卒婴城叛，邻郡多乘时科歛，官吏将效之，公弗听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1255515_comment'></div>至以利害怵，公坚不为动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1255515_comment'></div>旋踵贼平，诸郡骚然，而建昌之人不知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1255515_comment'></div>先是，禁旅阙，以故事选州卒之丁壮者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1255515_comment'></div>檄至郡，郡兵不肯去乡里，至流言相惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1255515_comment'></div>公独条上其事，朝廷是之，命姑毋至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1255515_comment'></div>江西建昌阜繁为一路剧，盗贼出没郊野为民患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1255515_comment'></div>公至，设方略，明赏罚，无问久近皆获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1255515_comment'></div>狱讼或累政不能决者，一问情辄得，郡中骇服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1255515_comment'></div>先是，造舟于溪，岁数毁，征诸往来者以赡其费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1255515_comment'></div>卒徒利其赢，至所取无艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1255515_comment'></div>公至，一切禁绝，且出库钱以更之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1255515_comment'></div>官鬻酒于民，强民之有婚丧者，公至悉罢除之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1255515_comment'></div>代还，百姓涕泣遮道，不忍其去云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1255515_comment'></div>绍兴乙亥岁，公六十有三矣，以是年四月十三日卒于湖州乌墩镇之寓舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1255515_comment'></div>公醇厚端靖，内外完好，心平而气舒，虽久处者未尝际其喜怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1255515_comment'></div>对宾客清谈亹亹，不及荣利，见者不自知其意之消也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1255515_comment'></div>閒居终日，襟抱冲澹，寂然若无意于世者，而中实明敏，遇事洞见无所遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1255515_comment'></div>为文援笔立成，典则而丽，读者厌服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1255515_comment'></div>家多蓄奇书，尽得其指归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1255515_comment'></div>平生操行过人，发于至诚，无毫发欺伪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1255515_comment'></div>虽家居澹泊，卒以济人利物为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1255515_comment'></div>每告戒子侄，即曰：「惟忠惟孝可以立身，惟廉惟慎可以涖官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1255515_comment'></div>吾自入仕，橐饘取给县官，每自反思所以称是者，未能也，汝曹其勉之」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1255515_comment'></div>与伯氏处，既老滋益恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1255515_comment'></div>始任子，舍其子耕老而官其兄之子，曰：「及吾兄之生存也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1255515_comment'></div>至公之殁，耕老犹未官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1255515_comment'></div>凡内外姻戚，赒其不足而字其无所归者，不为戚疏之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1255515_comment'></div>尝曰：「我常欲买田数百亩为义田，尽收宗族之贫者，以毕吾志，吾家非所忧也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1255515_comment'></div>其为郡无暴政，无矫情，以清静为治，所至晏然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1255515_comment'></div>平生不问生产，身虽宦达，所以自奉不异为书生时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1255515_comment'></div>去郡而归，橐无馀金，居无尺椽，寓居环堵之下，湫隘嚣尘，若不可堪忍，而公安之泊如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1255515_comment'></div>早岁通六经，至老探颐益深，而尤覃思于《易》，贯穿孔孟，出入释老，以求其所自得者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1255515_comment'></div>每一会意，信容得色晬然见于外，汲汲相告语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1255515_comment'></div>盖所志者，治心修身之要，非若俗儒猎取华采，为文章而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1255515_comment'></div>病革时，公之婿宋某开说云云，公曰：「了此久矣，毋多言」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1255515_comment'></div>盖其所以处死生者如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1255515_comment'></div>公之所居，乡邻爱之，虽庸夫贱隶无异辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1255515_comment'></div>闻其殁，往往太息泣下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1255515_comment'></div>夫人安吉朱氏，先公卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1255515_comment'></div>男一人，耕老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1255515_comment'></div>女二人：长适宋某，公姊子也，尝以进士举于乡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1255515_comment'></div>次适林森，业进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1255515_comment'></div>其家卜以某年某月某日葬于湖州英感山之阳，从君志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1255515_comment'></div>且属某状公行事，将以谒诸能文之士而铭诸幽，乃次比而授之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1255515_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_77_1255515_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年4月</a>　程克俊知湖州，上启致贺。作品：《贺新湖州程枢密启》<div id='poem_1255481' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255481' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255481?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺新湖州程枢密启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255481")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255481_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255481'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255481'>伏审起从真馆，荣镇辅藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255481_comment'></div>抚熊轼以班条，方耸一圻之望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255481_comment'></div>弹貂冠而就道，实归四海之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255481_comment'></div>凡在门阑，举皆抃蹈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255481_comment'></div>恭惟某官材任王佐，言为帝谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255481_comment'></div>利器无前，颖若万金之宝剑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255481_comment'></div>直躬不倚，凛如千尺之乔松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255481_comment'></div>心胸罗星斗之华，舌颊振风雷之厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255481_comment'></div>奋髯抵几，议论得其本根；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255481_comment'></div>掷简摇毫，文章盖其馀事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255481_comment'></div>素负经纶之业，特深旒扆之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255481_comment'></div>周旋视草之清班，密勿面槐之正席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255481_comment'></div>幄筹默运，助成不杀之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255481_comment'></div>枢柄密操，力赞有成之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255481_comment'></div>俄逐真庭之逸，遂谐仙里之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255481_comment'></div>寓直太平，孰若我公之最久？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255481_comment'></div>受釐宣室，果闻天子之见思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255481_comment'></div>方深图旧之谋，式赞维新之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255481_comment'></div>将入持于宰柄，始暂析于州符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255481_comment'></div>幕府将开，地接日图之近；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255481_comment'></div>驺从始戒，已传天语之温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255481_comment'></div>曾不俟于下车，亟借筹于前箸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255481_comment'></div>柱石之待元老，方倾侧席之求；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255481_comment'></div>衮绣以归我公，深切具瞻之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255481_comment'></div>某琐庸无取，历落多奇，早窥家有之书，莫逮庭趋之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255481_comment'></div>腼颜场屋，已坠世科；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255481_comment'></div>俯首簿书，尚尘官使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255481_comment'></div>邈矣清流之远，居然俗吏之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255481_comment'></div>重念某获出高门，最先多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255481_comment'></div>昔元老傅潜邸之日，在晚生偕胄子之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255481_comment'></div>方当未冠之年，已出提衡之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255481_comment'></div>宁为鸡口，仅成小战之名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1255481_comment'></div>先啖牛心，遂借虚声之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1255481_comment'></div>射石为虎，再发已穷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1255481_comment'></div>拔翼傅鳨，群飞则殆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1255481_comment'></div>年运而往，寖惊齿发之早衰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1255481_comment'></div>岁计有馀，更觉诗书之可乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1255481_comment'></div>益厌有求之谬，退思至当之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1255481_comment'></div>忧患相仍，况销精锐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1255481_comment'></div>田园半没，遂逐斗升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1255481_comment'></div>髀里肉生，叹初心之已负；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1255481_comment'></div>酒后耳热，知壮志之犹存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1255481_comment'></div>何出心迹之两歧，自觉语言之无味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1255481_comment'></div>听除书之传播，耸懦志以激昂，松竹相亲，久自安于困踬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1255481_comment'></div>李桃犹在，况旧出于栽培。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1255481_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年5月</a>　汤思退除知枢密院事，又上启致贺，祈求援引。作品：《贺汤知院启》<div id='poem_1255473' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255473' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255473?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺汤知院启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255473")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255473_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255473'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255473'>伏审光膺中旨，进位上枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255473_comment'></div>庙略纵横，久属苍生之望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255473_comment'></div>诏音深阔，益隆师尹之瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255473_comment'></div>风声所加，朝野交重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255473_comment'></div>窃以文武之备，本出于相须；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255473_comment'></div>军国之容，固由于一律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255473_comment'></div>国家复祖宗之旧，列辅弼之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255473_comment'></div>置左右之相，以交总于政机；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255473_comment'></div>列东西之府，以分董于戎事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255473_comment'></div>安如鼎足之峙，备若台符之联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255473_comment'></div>维时豪英，首被图任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255473_comment'></div>恭惟某官伟材经世，钜业代天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255473_comment'></div>廉拆以清美，若正音之播；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255473_comment'></div>温润而泽粲，如良玉之陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255473_comment'></div>翕为吾道之宗，允作斯文之倡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255473_comment'></div>掇异科而占等，阶迩列以升华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255473_comment'></div>翰苑专崇，独号禁中之颇、牧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255473_comment'></div>文衡屡秉，数逢闇里之曹、刘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255473_comment'></div>果从共政之巍班，奄宅本兵之正席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255473_comment'></div>筹合上意，宜有吾子房之褒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255473_comment'></div>名动远方，固多彼李揆之对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255473_comment'></div>雅闻诸将之尽服，无复一军之皆惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255473_comment'></div>忠谨不欺，以冕旒为知己；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255473_comment'></div>妖讹自息，知庙堂之有人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255473_comment'></div>俎豆军旅之事兼闻之，太尉、丞相之尊盖等耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255473_comment'></div>方共期于涣号，即大正于鼎司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255473_comment'></div>俯前后之三三，已践斗宫之秘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255473_comment'></div>参上下之两两，合从台铉之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255473_comment'></div>某结约无奇，嵚崎可笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255473_comment'></div>早游场屋，滥随俊造之后尘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255473_comment'></div>晚困簿书，获陪州县之下列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255473_comment'></div>邈矣清流之远，居然俗吏之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1255473_comment'></div>屡从松竹之游，未免稻粱之迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1255473_comment'></div>顾惟极陋，可谓至穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1255473_comment'></div>髀里肉生，叹初心之已负；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1255473_comment'></div>酒后耳热，觉壮志之尚存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1255473_comment'></div>窃自念于琐庸，尝早承于盼睐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1255473_comment'></div>缅怀二父，同登千佛之题；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1255473_comment'></div>藐是孤生，谓托两家之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1255473_comment'></div>每自忘于位貌，犹曲记于姓名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1255473_comment'></div>得意垣涂，尚作飞黄之顾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1255473_comment'></div>程工永夜，愿分邻烛之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1255473_comment'></div>病颡傥辱于系羁，焦尾或加之朴斲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1255473_comment'></div>三折肱之久，敢自列于平生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1255473_comment'></div>一引手之劳，方有望于门下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1255473_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1255473_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年6月</a>　程克俊拜参知政事，上启致贺，再求引荐。作品：《贺程参政启》<div id='poem_1255477' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255477' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255477?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺程参政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255477")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255477_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255477'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255477'>伏审光膺命綍，入与政机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255477_comment'></div>庙略纵横，久属苍生之望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255477_comment'></div>诏音深润，益隆师尹之瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255477_comment'></div>风声所加，朝野交庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255477_comment'></div>恭惟某官伟材经世，钜业格天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255477_comment'></div>廉折以清，美若正音之播；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255477_comment'></div>温润而泽，粲如良玉之陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255477_comment'></div>翕为吾道之宗，允作斯文之倡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255477_comment'></div>自翱翔于近密，最绵历于岁时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255477_comment'></div>晚从翰墨之清班，旋宅枢机之要地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255477_comment'></div>敛七兵于兰锜，助成不杀之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255477_comment'></div>还百姓于锄犁，尽获有生之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255477_comment'></div>名遂而退，功成不居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255477_comment'></div>养重望于乡闾，十有三载；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255477_comment'></div>播英声于海宇，万口一辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255477_comment'></div>威名闻草木之知，姓字入儿童之诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255477_comment'></div>果趣介圭之觐，且留千乘之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255477_comment'></div>顾公行勿迟，共致邦人之祝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255477_comment'></div>然外论不尔，方倾海宇之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255477_comment'></div>当圣神亲总于万机，而辅弼备列于三省，允极一道之选，倚成万世之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255477_comment'></div>维时耆英，首被图任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255477_comment'></div>不见贾生之久，自勤宣室之思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255477_comment'></div>毋以我公之归，徒有东山之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255477_comment'></div>方共期于涣号，即大正于鼎司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255477_comment'></div>某结约无奇，嵚崎可笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255477_comment'></div>早失庭趋之训，粗窥家有之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255477_comment'></div>偶失足于世科，逐寄身于吏禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255477_comment'></div>驰驱州县，荏苒岁时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255477_comment'></div>屡从松竹之游，未免稻粱之迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255477_comment'></div>重念某甫登冠岁，已出高门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255477_comment'></div>程艺文衡，处以诸生之右；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255477_comment'></div>剡章黼扆，借之一字之褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1255477_comment'></div>自黾勉于一官，忽侵寻于七闰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1255477_comment'></div>顾无成之若此，岂有命之使然！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1255477_comment'></div>腼颜若自于己知，殁齿忍居于人后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1255477_comment'></div>靖思愚陋，宜在弃捐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1255477_comment'></div>顷因尺牍之修，略叙寸心之蕴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1255477_comment'></div>随关听览，傥辱哀怜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1255477_comment'></div>皂盖翻翻，已处帡幪之下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1255477_comment'></div>衮衣奕奕，更居埏埴之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1255477_comment'></div>自欣幸会之逢，辄写悃悰之素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1255477_comment'></div>曳裾相望，曾莫与于后陈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1255477_comment'></div>坠履见收，或兴怜于旧物。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1255477_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年4月</a>　在湖州长兴县丞任上。强行父卒，为撰行状。作品：《右中散大夫提举台州崇道观强公行状》<div id='poem_1255516' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255516' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255516?labeling=true' target='_blank'>右中散大夫提举台州崇道观强公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255516")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255516_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255516'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255516'>公讳某，字幼安，钱塘人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255516_comment'></div>皇曾祖讳冲，隐德不仕，累赠尚书职方员外郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255516_comment'></div>妣程氏，封仙源县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255516_comment'></div>皇祖讳至，始以进士起家，终尚书祠部郎中、三司户部判官，以子贵赠金紫光禄大夫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255516_comment'></div>妣杨氏、曾氏，封吴、鲁郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255516_comment'></div>皇考讳俊明，历尚书主客员外郎，终两浙路提点刑狱，以公贵赠开府仪同三司；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255516_comment'></div>妣赵氏，封荣国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255516_comment'></div>强氏之先，其别自齐，盖本姜姓，班班见于汉、唐、苻秦之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255516_comment'></div>至国朝，公之祖考始以文学大显，为世称首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255516_comment'></div>公尤警敏，四岁能辨四声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255516_comment'></div>年十有五而孤，太夫人相继即世，刻意问学，居乡数年，人罕识面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255516_comment'></div>从乡先生施国光学，遇讲解，尝默记数千言，退而笔之，无一脱遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255516_comment'></div>齿最少，同辈敬惮，不敢为逸游慢戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255516_comment'></div>开府公嗜学，博极百氏，造次未始释卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255516_comment'></div>公从旁观之，悉能记忆，问辄响答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255516_comment'></div>馆客傅崧卿子骏极爱重之，叔父文宪公渊明尤器焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255516_comment'></div>居乡最为乡人所推，薛太尉昂目为后进第一，李修撰及闻而敬爱，与为忘年交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255516_comment'></div>未冠，以开府公恩补太庙斋郎，调睦州遂安县兼主簿，时年二十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255516_comment'></div>持身廉约，一介不以取人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255516_comment'></div>滞讼有越十年者付公，一言决之，一邑称服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255516_comment'></div>民有方泽者，讼前令，去之，亟输粟得官以自庇，横益甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255516_comment'></div>士子郭霖、邵振民之徒，持吏短长，以自衣食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255516_comment'></div>公来，皆屏息悔过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255516_comment'></div>时朝廷重兴州县学宫，吏奉行唯谨，闾阎氓隶假逢掖立讼庭，则长吏改容加礼，事无曲直，一切右之，不则叫号欢呶，或面骂不顾，令不能制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255516_comment'></div>值公在坐，则循循如平时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255516_comment'></div>以是公旦旦造令，讼未毕不听去也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255516_comment'></div>有詹天申者稍不逊，公遣人谕以理，少选，詹之族长相率携天申诣公愧谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255516_comment'></div>公因勉励之，卒为善士，后登科，仕为升朝官云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255516_comment'></div>县岁给蚕盐，豪民劫持强取，多或倍蓰，吏破产以偿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255516_comment'></div>公命工织竹为畚者百馀，细大有差，预实之，乱其钞而覆置之，次第而赋，讫事无敢哗者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255516_comment'></div>吏以手加额曰：「使官得宰天下，当如此盐矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255516_comment'></div>未几，移长洲尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1255516_comment'></div>过市，民皆啜泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1255516_comment'></div>后十有九年，以避地复来，士民争出劳问，相与调护焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1255516_comment'></div>时去乱未几，邑豪杰更为长雄，乱屡起，令姑息不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1255516_comment'></div>公适寓居，犹以遗爱得其欢心，岁时问遗，邑人赖以为安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1255516_comment'></div>又尝之淳安，遣仆市药于肆，主人潜益其数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1255516_comment'></div>公觉而归之，不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1255516_comment'></div>县吏见之，叱使去，曰：「是尝官吾邻邑，唯井水不以钱取，汝曹无知，敢污若人耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1255516_comment'></div>及为长洲尉，守盛章恃势恣横，郡官多谄以求进，小忤意，中以危法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1255516_comment'></div>公从容有常，章敬爱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1255516_comment'></div>既去，称誉不衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1255516_comment'></div>未几，除主管编估局，既而复改刬刷折钞官物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1255516_comment'></div>时文宪公年高多病，跬步不许离侍侧，而折钞官例不坐曹，如公之志云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1255516_comment'></div>改承奉郎，除光禄寺丞，兼大晟府杂务官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1255516_comment'></div>踰年，文宪公薨，除公通判杭州，年二十六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1255516_comment'></div>人初少之，而公遇事敏明，老吏皆畏服，以为不可及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1255516_comment'></div>杭本乡郡，公持身廉平，亲旧来者礼之，馈者厚报之，恩意往来如平时，皆得其欢心，然终不敢以毫发私慁公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1255516_comment'></div>杭为一都会，多奸盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1255516_comment'></div>吏薛昌以善迹捕名里中，昌弟宁桀骜横一方，州郡倚以为用，虽名太守莫敢诘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1255516_comment'></div>每捕弗满品，即推一无赖者，号家人，代之受责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1255516_comment'></div>公取其牒视之，曰：「姓名汝也，又奚辞」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1255516_comment'></div>即属吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1255516_comment'></div>宁惶惧，愿自效，公不听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1255516_comment'></div>昌走白太守，守知公不可夺，卒杖之，诸薛为少衰，良民以安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1255516_comment'></div>吏马端者，专掌鞫狱，一州侧目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1255516_comment'></div>公行守事，端来不以时，命数卒捽置庭下，痛捶之，市人称快，迄公去，不敢为奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1255516_comment'></div>公所决讼，人多纪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1255516_comment'></div>后方腊陷杭州，族僧法秀者，老而有戒行，方逃伏山中，以书抵公曰：「州人出万死，犹谈强寺丞断事不去口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1255516_comment'></div>到今郡人语及公，必以手加额」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1255516_comment'></div>陈通据城叛，尤嫉衣冠，公出入兵间，皆起立致恭云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1255516_comment'></div>初，公在杭，待制赵公㠓来典是州，公外诸翁也，不敢以儿子畜公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1255516_comment'></div>赵雅饰厨传，一日偕郡僚登双门，曰：「官奴殊未差择」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1255516_comment'></div>将属公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1255516_comment'></div>公举手谢不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1255516_comment'></div>且曰：「非某事，有仪曹在」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1255516_comment'></div>赵愠见而罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1255516_comment'></div>其他规正多此类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1255516_comment'></div>然心爱公，尝语人曰：「吾内外族之贤者，霈与幼安二人而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1255516_comment'></div>霈，赵兄子也，后为工部侍郎云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1255516_comment'></div>公在职多馀暇，数游西湖两山间及龙山诸刹，与文人秀士论文赋诗，及高僧逸人为方外之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1255516_comment'></div>每出行县，迹遍历胜处，徜徉兼旬乃归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1255516_comment'></div>当是时，权倖用事，其党皆据在州要职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1255516_comment'></div>或衔命出入，每会集，金带烂然照坐，在仕者多结以媒进，有骤用者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1255516_comment'></div>公未尝与之亲昵，然不得而怨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1255516_comment'></div>给事中傅公墨卿使高丽，取道钱塘归，语其弟崧卿曰：「方是时，某亦不能处之使如此，盖惟有道者能之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1255516_comment'></div>及终更，爱公者以书私相贺曰：「强幼安完璧而归，可喜也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1255516_comment'></div>公初佐徐端明铸，独泊然无附意，日一见，非公事未尝请间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1255516_comment'></div>官欲满而徐去，过公，太息曰：「某尝接前辈，如公似之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1255516_comment'></div>公去年受代时，居舍在城西，蒿莱没人，而邸店别业率颓毁不治，盖未尝役一匠者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1255516_comment'></div>某心服焉，始知徐初不敢以众人见遇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1255516_comment'></div>罢官去京师，寓景德寺，与眉山唐子西以文字相酬酢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1255516_comment'></div>子西夜过公，语或到钟鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1255516_comment'></div>时宰相谢宾客，有劝公诡道以求见者，公谢不愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1255516_comment'></div>久之，得通判宣州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1255516_comment'></div>杭倅选甚高，前此未有复为倅者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1255516_comment'></div>公至宣州，守俞公焘旧好饮燕，不事事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1255516_comment'></div>公到，数辞疾不往，守为之稍损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1255516_comment'></div>事有与法戾者，必从容规正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1255516_comment'></div>时州方建神霄宫，忠翊郎徐正德护宫门戟幡由京师来，自谓童贯门人，守畏权势，礼之如王人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1255516_comment'></div>倨益甚，郊迓数里外，称疾不得见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1255516_comment'></div>公适到郡，吏白致书，不听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1255516_comment'></div>既视事，问戟何为不立，曰：「奉使有命，须病间」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1255516_comment'></div>公曰：「此在选使臣尔，护戟到州，无他虞职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1255516_comment'></div>奉安乃州郡事，彼何与」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1255516_comment'></div>守不听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1255516_comment'></div>公命一戎官即舟次，谕以新通判意，曰：「戟到久不立，岂朝廷崇奉之意？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1255516_comment'></div>今择日奉安，倘管押官病未间，持假状来」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1255516_comment'></div>正德皇恐，力疾出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1255516_comment'></div>正德既自他郡回，曰：「童宣抚命我市物，为钱若干，须车以载」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1255516_comment'></div>公使索文檄阅视，且问费将安取，语塞不能报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1255516_comment'></div>会部使者来，犹据传舍不肯避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1255516_comment'></div>公遣牙卒二十辈迁之僧舍，明日遂行，众论快服，时宣和二年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1255516_comment'></div>是年十月，盗方腊发睦州青溪县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1255516_comment'></div>十一月，稍逼新安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1255516_comment'></div>知歙州曾公孝蕴移帅营丘，知宣州上官公敦复老而畏愞，亟求去，得提举江西常平，知广德军韩公某亦以老病自列罢去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1255516_comment'></div>三州皆以通判行守事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1255516_comment'></div>而宣、歙接壤，唇齿之国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1255516_comment'></div>贼势日张，承平岁久，民不知兵，远近汹惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1255516_comment'></div>闻之朝廷，辄寝不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1255516_comment'></div>江东帅司遣东南第三将，西人号病关索者，老于行阵，慨然有平贼志，然其所统乃江东诸郡兵尔，皆恇怯不习战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1255516_comment'></div>驻军歙州，贼率众来犯，亟帅所部应之，身冒矢石，为士卒先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1255516_comment'></div>未战，众皆溃，将死之，贼遂陷绩溪，宣州大震。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1255516_comment'></div>先是，御笔以江东漕李侗董率诸州兵讨贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1255516_comment'></div>侗，宣人也，领江宁兵八百人驰赴山前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1255516_comment'></div>既到宣，闻歙已危，顿兵不进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1255516_comment'></div>公方缮城壁，募敢勇为守御计，分遣巡尉扼其要冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1255516_comment'></div>有摄管界巡检张禹臣者，自言将家子，愿自效，请往杭、宣境上，气锐甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1255516_comment'></div>行三舍抵宁国，闻歙已陷，驻溪南僧寺不进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1255516_comment'></div>中夜凭高远觇，如有火光然，大惧，委众驰还，所过以策叩门，大呼曰：「寇来矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1255516_comment'></div>五鼓抵城下，径造宣城县及使漕幕府言状，且云：「贼壁南门矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1255516_comment'></div>公使状其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1255516_comment'></div>既又走南陵云：「贼临青弋江矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1255516_comment'></div>江去县不能五十里，于是城中官吏百姓尽室奔窜，一城为空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1255516_comment'></div>公亟诣漕计事，则既装矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1255516_comment'></div>方退，则已领众出北门，趋江宁，于是内外大扰，寇攘蜂起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1255516_comment'></div>先是，漕使取太平州诸县土兵弓手一百五十人自随，是日抵宣州，漕以州无兵以畀公，公使分护帑廪囹圄，而州禁卒调发溃散，才馀三十六人，各给兵仗，列在庭下，目为亲兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1255516_comment'></div>当是时，官吏无复一人存，独公在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1255516_comment'></div>骑诣诸狱，慰抚囚之在禁者，又走帑廪，坏扃鐍，以给士卒之仰哺者，亟遣人往宁国问状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1255516_comment'></div>邑尉来告，境内无寇，昨夕贫民附火耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1255516_comment'></div>公访得一二小吏，求纸笔书榜以告百姓，将乘时作乱，公觉之，不为动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1255516_comment'></div>入夜，城中四面次第纵火，从者襆被持马促公去者数四，云：「贼已入城纵火，不可少俟」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1255516_comment'></div>公诡对曰：「吾决矣，姑更觇其实」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1255516_comment'></div>乃遣人之火所，既又报火方起，则又遣一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1255516_comment'></div>乃解衣就寝，戒老卒曰：「吾夙兴罢甚，觇者至，俟来晨并白」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1255516_comment'></div>于是投床大鼾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1255516_comment'></div>众知不可动，不复言火矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1255516_comment'></div>翌日，州监军宣城宰始自城外还，胥徒亦有归者，百姓诉剽夺者相属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1255516_comment'></div>公捕得，命荷以大校，帽其首如大辟者，书其械以徇于郊外，曰：「将不以常法治之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1255516_comment'></div>于是人始知惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1255516_comment'></div>宣州自政和末病水，流徙者十室而九，存者无以自赡，及是肆掠居民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1255516_comment'></div>宣城宰出，民持檄赴愬，遮道不得行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1255516_comment'></div>宰以白公，公命吏视其居处，以类相从，书其后以付巡尉，戒以须生致毋擅取首级，非格斗毋轻用矢刃，非经有司鞫实不以论赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1255516_comment'></div>于是鸣金鼓献俘者早晚不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1255516_comment'></div>公命列之于庭，挟以铠仗，乃出据厅事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1255516_comment'></div>士卒有功，赏以金钱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1255516_comment'></div>里正若土豪与有力者，劳给加等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1255516_comment'></div>延巡尉坐语，温言相劳苦，然后以贼付有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1255516_comment'></div>人人喜悦自奋，未旬日，奸人屏息，境内肃然安堵，城中外户不闭，见道遗者辄连呼其人，授之然后去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1255516_comment'></div>先是，城孤兵寡，度贼到无以守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1255516_comment'></div>有周某者，自言有家徒三百，膂力绝人，愿率以捍城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1255516_comment'></div>官吏得之欣然，请借兵资粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1255516_comment'></div>公独疑之，命赴宣城县问状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1255516_comment'></div>周请与弓级蒋彬者偕行，彬一见，唾骂曰：「县官何负汝，乃欲反乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1255516_comment'></div>若顷为强盗，吾获汝，欲杀我甘心耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1255516_comment'></div>周抚膺惭恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1255516_comment'></div>宰阳怒彬，叱使去，好言谕周：「诘旦以尔诣州，为汝请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1255516_comment'></div>是夕大扰，失周所在，乃径出村落为盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1255516_comment'></div>里正率众围之，格杀周，搜其衣间有降书，将举城以应贼者，盖独惮蒋彬，欲先以计取之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1255516_comment'></div>方是时，非公先见，城几殆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1255516_comment'></div>漕宪讽公清野，及焚附城民居积聚，公曰：「是非边城比，内外皆吾民，奈何弃之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1255516_comment'></div>是时，州县察奸甚密，城门昼闭，商旅不得行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1255516_comment'></div>公曰：「贼所为遣间侦伺者，以未测吾虚实也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1255516_comment'></div>今吾州无城与民，孰不知之，何以侦为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1255516_comment'></div>重扰吾民，无益也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1255516_comment'></div>命勿察，城门启闭如无事时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1255516_comment'></div>间与同僚置酒高会，赋诗为乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1255516_comment'></div>敌罔测，不敢轻犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1255516_comment'></div>自军兴，州县多便宜杀戮以威众，公独不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1255516_comment'></div>张禹臣晚自归，众谓当斩以徇，否则械系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1255516_comment'></div>公曰：「某人臣也，何得专杀？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1255516_comment'></div>且一命以上荷校有著令」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1255516_comment'></div>第付狱奏劾而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1255516_comment'></div>虽捕获奸盗，必问法何如，不自为轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1255516_comment'></div>时取一二死囚，断其首竿于市，远近骇服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1255516_comment'></div>事闻京师，执政者拊掌惊叹，曰：「儒者之勇也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1255516_comment'></div>宣为江淮襟喉，贼得宣则江淮横溃，为京师忧，是以时多比公于巡、远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1255516_comment'></div>尽明年正月，朝廷方起钱公即为守，大军亦踵来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1255516_comment'></div>二月五日，庐州队将田某与三州巡检黄𧦬与贼战麾岭下，大败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1255516_comment'></div>贼陷宁国，直抵黄社，距州城四十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1255516_comment'></div>时东兵将夏仔相继率众一千五百人趋宁国，闻败不救，领兵径还，夜抵城外，莫知为贼为官军也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1255516_comment'></div>守惧，与漕使俱出北门，欲趋太平州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1255516_comment'></div>公亟自出城追及，谕以利害，与俱还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1255516_comment'></div>贼闻大军且到，旁趋旌德，州城复安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1255516_comment'></div>当是时，童贯出为统帅，思所以为归报藉手者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1255516_comment'></div>广德军有常平钱六万埋地中，军倅取以献，贯大悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1255516_comment'></div>或以此讽公，公曰：「军兴，州县所费无艺，更以为献，将不免科调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1255516_comment'></div>为一身计可尔，如吾民重困何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1255516_comment'></div>言者愧服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1255516_comment'></div>然贯由是不乐，及第功，他郡倅获厚赏，州守钱公就加龙图阁学士，而不及公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1255516_comment'></div>钱初欲论于朝，其子谏之，畏祸而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1255516_comment'></div>是时，帅臣监司咸欲为公言之，士民亦为公讼功不已，而漕以屡跳为耻，众相视莫敢发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1255516_comment'></div>然欲默不忍，各以著令荐员举公，其词则极道城守事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1255516_comment'></div>内翰徐公绩以书抵公，曰：「仁者有勇，今见之矣，碌碌鼠辈不足道也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1255516_comment'></div>盖指侗辈云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1255516_comment'></div>西州士人屈通从军过宣州，摭民言为《楚歌》二十章，其末皆云「我不去」，盖实录也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1255516_comment'></div>其馀作为语言以记一时之功者甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1255516_comment'></div>童贯既班师，宣有四大寇环处境内，合散出没，四郊骚然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1255516_comment'></div>州檄公督捕，久之悉平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1255516_comment'></div>先是，诸州捕贼得辄杀，不问其所由来，良民往往为贼坚守巢穴，屡拒官军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1255516_comment'></div>公请于宣抚司，悬赏募为首及用事者，胁从一切置不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1255516_comment'></div>又与帅约，无遣将兵，喜扰而善惊，用之适足败事，在道者还之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1255516_comment'></div>但会数县巡尉及召募勇敢士分布要路，戒以无得妄出兵，且谕巡尉曰：「吾曹第为国家毕事，毋贪功幸赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1255516_comment'></div>他时有赏，通判不专有也，多寡当与诸君均之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1255516_comment'></div>乃镂板为榜百纸，募人持入贼中，揭道上，众稍离叛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1255516_comment'></div>间有执贼来者，问知胁从，立慰遣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1255516_comment'></div>于是徒党尽散，独所谓首领用事者数辈，窜伏山谷，未几皆擒获无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1255516_comment'></div>公迁官一等，巡尉第赏有差，如初约焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1255516_comment'></div>公之以职事留郊外也，一日得部使者檄，以朝旨委公，密具弃城官吏姓名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1255516_comment'></div>方公摄事，时郡官皆出境外，间有驰归者，闻一虚传即日去，或白事未竟，就坐潜遁，虽主兵官亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1255516_comment'></div>皆盘泊和、太平、真、扬、高邮，逮事平始归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1255516_comment'></div>同时守会稽者，劾弃城官吏，皆荷校远窜，守骤加职数等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1255516_comment'></div>公念事出意表，安能人人责其固守，独守臣不可去尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1255516_comment'></div>人情不相远，使数十百家流离狼狈，己取厚赏，安乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1255516_comment'></div>即报以无弃城者，僚属由是获免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1255516_comment'></div>初，郡官闻有檄，忧惧不知所出，候公入城，迎叩公，犹相视怀疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1255516_comment'></div>公命取案牍示之，无不感服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1255516_comment'></div>关注子东作序送行，具载其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1255516_comment'></div>钱公号风力帅，所到不假僚吏以权，独重公为，政事无细大，一皆诹访。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1255516_comment'></div>文书经公者、钱不复省视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1255516_comment'></div>尝行县，郡事留不决以待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1255516_comment'></div>然其为人尚威猛，下情或不得通，公介居其间以济之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1255516_comment'></div>钱尝云：「公之处事，初若不快人意，徐而思之，莫不曲当，盖某所不及也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1255516_comment'></div>倅宣二年，领郡事者十七八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1255516_comment'></div>比去，民闭门遮道，不听去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1255516_comment'></div>公去踰一纪，宣州吏卒时犹为讹言相动云：「强寺丞来守此州」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1255516_comment'></div>踊跃驩呼，以先睹为快。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1255516_comment'></div>公之友黄公子鲁自新安之建康，道宣州溪上，饭于野店，一妪前问曰：「官识强寺丞否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1255516_comment'></div>今安在」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1255516_comment'></div>曰：「在馀杭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1255516_comment'></div>「安否」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1255516_comment'></div>曰：「安」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1255516_comment'></div>则以手加额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1255516_comment'></div>黄曰：「汝何为问之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1255516_comment'></div>曰：「若人，宣民再生父母也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1255516_comment'></div>自有吾州以来，得知州、通判、知县才各一人，此其人也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1255516_comment'></div>问守为谁，曰李龙图，令曰李朝奉，盖光、椿年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1255516_comment'></div>公始还乡里，造父友傅岩老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1255516_comment'></div>迎劳曰：「宣城之节甚高，行季有子矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1255516_comment'></div>行季，开府公字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1255516_comment'></div>杨公时一见公，大奇之，曰：「强氏有此人」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1255516_comment'></div>一时名胜，造门愿交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1255516_comment'></div>入朝，道毗陵，钱公谢事家居，宾客不得通，闻公在门，肩舆亟出，留连欢甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1255516_comment'></div>曰：「公之为政，吏师也，有德又有言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1255516_comment'></div>老夫退居静念，愈觉可服」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1255516_comment'></div>是时王黼当轴，官以贿成，因曰：「闻迩来官有定价，非是不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1255516_comment'></div>公奕世清德，其值不赀，宁不得官，慎勿为此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1255516_comment'></div>公敛衽谢曰：「某素心也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1255516_comment'></div>留毂下半年，果不得官，乃告去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1255516_comment'></div>居乡二年，殆无出仕意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1255516_comment'></div>亲故更劝勉，乃再趋朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1255516_comment'></div>诣吏部，视文榜有湖州司录事者，即求以归，时论为之扼腕，而公恬然自若也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1255516_comment'></div>杨公时屡为蔡攸辈言之，不效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1255516_comment'></div>公于蔡氏虽姻戚，然未尝少为之屈，故不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1255516_comment'></div>及其将败也，攸子衎除徽猷阁直学士，始荐自代，虽其父祖犹以为然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1255516_comment'></div>唐公恪、许公景衡，相知尤笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1255516_comment'></div>会渊圣即位，二公方向用，慨然许以振起，及执政辄忘之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1255516_comment'></div>盖公耻于自售，故难进如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1255516_comment'></div>公方待次里中，会朝廷穷治朱勔党与，命江浙漕臣凡以勔得官者即斥之，莫知主名，则求勔故吏，俾疏姓氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1255516_comment'></div>由是争夺纷纷，或讦以自售，而公之代者亦误堕罢中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1255516_comment'></div>檄既去矣，一日漕使招公甚急，面授檄使之官，仍戒以速行毋留，且有所畀付。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1255516_comment'></div>公力明其不然，曰：「閒居六年，宁不急禄，然岂可厚诬他人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1255516_comment'></div>不敢承命」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1255516_comment'></div>漕再三勉谕，辞益坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1255516_comment'></div>以公言为信然，乃已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1255516_comment'></div>既而代者始使人自辨，然事已白矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1255516_comment'></div>当是时，犹用旧制，圭田以四月三十日为断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1255516_comment'></div>月既望，漕以此动公，曰：「藉彼不然，而文移往来，犹可易朔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1255516_comment'></div>公辞不愿，漕终身愧服，士论益以此归重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1255516_comment'></div>公未到吴兴，郡守直龙图阁梁公端闻公名，悚然以待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1255516_comment'></div>时钱塘叛军尚婴城，湖卒董照等亦谋据城叛，其党以告，为首者孥戮之，郡僚迁秩一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1255516_comment'></div>于是州下令诸营卒十人为一保，一人有谋，十家坐之，又联城中居民为保伍以伺察，军士反侧不自安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1255516_comment'></div>而公适到郡，有兵士张青者，夜梯子城西门，并茶肆，登屋纵火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1255516_comment'></div>未及燃，为保伍所执，一城汹汹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1255516_comment'></div>质明，守命理官鞫于郡圃，具得纵火状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1255516_comment'></div>因会郡僚议罪，皆曰当如约束，戮十家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1255516_comment'></div>公曰：「不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1255516_comment'></div>前日孥戮，出于仓卒，不暇详议，然何可为常？<div class='inline'
