id='poem_sentence_277_1255516_comment'></div>今日之事，唯宽可以已乱，不然众怒不可遏，此州殆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1255516_comment'></div>且焉知斯人于彼不有私憾，未见反状，当傅轻典」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1255516_comment'></div>同列曰：「唯前日用刑太恕，无人忌惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1255516_comment'></div>若更从轻，则乱可立俟」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1255516_comment'></div>公固争曰：「杀人不是好事，须宽猛迭用，不然人人思乱矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1255516_comment'></div>守独谓公曰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1255516_comment'></div>「幼安与某意合，然则当如何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_284_1255516_comment'></div>公曰：「烧有人居舍，在法当死，况当此时，且近子城，处以极典，夫复何辞」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_285_1255516_comment'></div>又问家属，曰：「徙邻州」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_286_1255516_comment'></div>又问十保人，曰：「杖而释之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_287_1255516_comment'></div>同列犹力争，守不听，退坐后厅，书断如公言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_288_1255516_comment'></div>未竟，客至，曰十保人已轻，因令俱徙邻州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_289_1255516_comment'></div>既命斩张青市中，薄暮始治馀人，登时迫遣上道，家属相送，哭声震野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_290_1255516_comment'></div>是夕卒辈无人色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_291_1255516_comment'></div>于是巡察益严，溪下小舟一一搜索不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_292_1255516_comment'></div>时方增置武尉，募新弓手二百人，州令分守武库，以备不虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_293_1255516_comment'></div>于是弓手横凌军士，军士愤怨，道遇新弓手辄殴之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_294_1255516_comment'></div>守一付公使治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_295_1255516_comment'></div>公呼證佐使前，曰：「彼均国家人也，州郡遇之无厚薄，但殴人者罪耳，汝当以实言，不然先罪汝」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_296_1255516_comment'></div>咸对以实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_297_1255516_comment'></div>又呼军士前，反覆问之，至三四，然后杖之，莫不悔服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_298_1255516_comment'></div>有龙骑节级陈方及舟师沈青，攘袂市中，曰：「吾必为死者复怨」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_299_1255516_comment'></div>一郡以为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_300_1255516_comment'></div>已而陈方遇一鬻青果者于涂，夺其刀揕之，伤胸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1255516_comment'></div>逻者录以送州，众皆喜，谓去此人有名矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_302_1255516_comment'></div>公私语守曰：「慎无急杀，一陈方易尔，然祸有不可胜讳者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_303_1255516_comment'></div>姑系狱，徐议之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_304_1255516_comment'></div>翌日，伤者困重，始荷以大校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_305_1255516_comment'></div>方举目直视，鼻息咈然，众益惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_306_1255516_comment'></div>已而其妻又诬鬻果者怨其夫，持刀逐己，众證不然，杖而遣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_307_1255516_comment'></div>于是杂然谓使方出狱必为乱，当遂去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_308_1255516_comment'></div>公曰：「法有限，候限至徐议区处尔，何遽也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_309_1255516_comment'></div>守呼法吏将改配，公曰：「改配亦逃归尔，何益」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_310_1255516_comment'></div>守问计于公，曰：「第付某决杖可也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_311_1255516_comment'></div>守孤疑虑累日，不得已，然公言，诸黥随之者数十百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_312_1255516_comment'></div>公初命依法行决，才数下，方号呼若不能堪者，遽命释之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_313_1255516_comment'></div>且使升阶，好谓曰：「吾视汝貌，岂碌碌者，异日立功名，享官爵，殆未可量，而轻生如此，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_314_1255516_comment'></div>使前日被伤者不幸遂死，汝且不免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_315_1255516_comment'></div>虽有富贵，将谁使享之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_316_1255516_comment'></div>太守兼管内安抚，岂不能以便宜斩汝？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_317_1255516_comment'></div>盖将责汝后效，吾又从而贷汝，亦知悔未也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_318_1255516_comment'></div>曰：「然」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_319_1255516_comment'></div>曰：「侥倖不再，而今而后，当自爱毋忽」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_320_1255516_comment'></div>方再拜谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_321_1255516_comment'></div>众卒欢呼，以手加额，曰：「官犹齿吾辈于人类乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_322_1255516_comment'></div>守初犹忧之，后半月见公，曰：「陈方帖然，公勉以忠义之力也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_323_1255516_comment'></div>未几，沈青又以私酿捕获，众持论如前日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_324_1255516_comment'></div>公曰：「不当与陈方异罚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_325_1255516_comment'></div>亦杖而释之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_326_1255516_comment'></div>自是湖卒不复萌反意，州人于今不见兵革，实公之功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_327_1255516_comment'></div>苗、刘肆逆，挟诏旨以除内侍，有寓他州者，辄没其家赀，徙之远方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_328_1255516_comment'></div>吴兴郡官一时受牒者数人，惟公处之得宜，毫发不使有欺隐，而其家以口赋服用饮食甚备，具名物归之案牍，曰：「此固诏旨也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_329_1255516_comment'></div>其人感泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_330_1255516_comment'></div>未几，有诏复给，于是诉者纷纷，而公独晏然，众又愈服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_331_1255516_comment'></div>在湖一年半，凡诉讼，守一委公，倅具员而已，郡无留事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_332_1255516_comment'></div>公所决，皆傅情法，无纤介私，州人思之不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_333_1255516_comment'></div>时公初脱兵革，囊中无留藏，独恃月俸，有馀辄分畀同事，郡守益以此多之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_334_1255516_comment'></div>公雅志退藏，见四方多故，遂挂衣冠去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_335_1255516_comment'></div>会新天子即位，用人如不及，翰林学士汪公藻等交荐，诏公主管亳州明道宫，除通判永州，改主管台州崇道观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_336_1255516_comment'></div>初秩满，除通判泉州，复改崇道祠事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_337_1255516_comment'></div>任满赴阙，望倾一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_338_1255516_comment'></div>凡论人物，必以公称首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_339_1255516_comment'></div>时有诏从官荐堪任监司郡守者，将书姓名御屏以待选用，观其治否以殿最举者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_340_1255516_comment'></div>又诏须明指事实，不得泛论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_341_1255516_comment'></div>又诏监司、郡守有阙，先除所荐人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_342_1255516_comment'></div>吏部侍郎晏公敦复、兵部侍郎刘公宁止、给事中傅公崧卿，以公应诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_343_1255516_comment'></div>傅雅器公，尝欲以十科荐，会资序碍格乃止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_344_1255516_comment'></div>为舍人时尝以所草赠告三十六道书以畀公，使书其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_345_1255516_comment'></div>前后屡荐，动辄数百言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_346_1255516_comment'></div>初以给事史官赐对，又反复口陈，不觉日旰，皇恐谢曰：「臣奏事喋喋，烦黩圣听」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_347_1255516_comment'></div>上曰：「不妨，正要如是」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_348_1255516_comment'></div>然与时宰无素，卒不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_349_1255516_comment'></div>乃从吏部调，签书平江军节度判官厅公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_350_1255516_comment'></div>到官，会郡守数易，倅白彦搆适行守事，性多苛而疏率，文书有不合理者，公辄持不肯下，虽力取之不为动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_351_1255516_comment'></div>既而出旁郡，以州事诿公者凡五十日，日阅讼牒千馀，区理郡事，一府厌服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_352_1255516_comment'></div>既而公诸舅徽猷阁直学士赵公霈来知府事，赵雅爱重公，日间见坐语堂上，老兵辈悉屏远，每事问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_353_1255516_comment'></div>公以忠厚信于上下，赵所施为，一事近厚，曰：「必自强丈出」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_354_1255516_comment'></div>不然则曰：「强丈未言尔，姑待之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_355_1255516_comment'></div>赵固劲正，公左右之，治状远闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_356_1255516_comment'></div>己未秋大旱，户部尚书梁汝嘉建言漕运不通，请下杭、湖、苏三州募游手二万人治漕河，自秀州抵长河堰凡一百八里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_357_1255516_comment'></div>公得之，笑曰：「彼初无水源，必待天泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_358_1255516_comment'></div>无益，第漕下塘可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_359_1255516_comment'></div>且岁旱井眢，万众野处，弱者暍死，壮者溃而归尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_360_1255516_comment'></div>移书言事官，罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_361_1255516_comment'></div>是日大雨踰二尺，漕运以通，汝嘉憾焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_362_1255516_comment'></div>吏部尚书张公焘、吏部侍郎刘公岑、给事中刘公一止、中书舍人李公谊，共荐公可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_363_1255516_comment'></div>惟焘遂及宣城城守事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_364_1255516_comment'></div>丞相曰单方择守，其以公往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_365_1255516_comment'></div>既而以私计辞行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_366_1255516_comment'></div>秩满，主管崇道观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_367_1255516_comment'></div>宰相秦益公既悉公行治，兵部侍郎程公瑀乘间道公姓名，秦闻之欣然，即除知常州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_368_1255516_comment'></div>始一识面，叹曰：「清苦之士也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_369_1255516_comment'></div>退而之郡，岁且旱，入境而雨告足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_370_1255516_comment'></div>自是凡有水旱，走群望，应不移晷，且间有异事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_371_1255516_comment'></div>公老于州郡，听决如流，虽毛密，应如有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_372_1255516_comment'></div>率以辰刻退食，未刻始复视事，迨晡休吏卒，当昼门庭阒然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_373_1255516_comment'></div>暇日书传皆自校勘，或手抄，其从容如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_374_1255516_comment'></div>为治简静，不事苛刻，人谓有前辈风度，上下安乐之，迄今士民思咏不去口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_375_1255516_comment'></div>贡献赂遗，一切罢去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_376_1255516_comment'></div>守臣供须，非法所有，一毫不取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_377_1255516_comment'></div>邻州馈饷，不以归私家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_378_1255516_comment'></div>会元夕，按乐行酒速，于是漕始大怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_379_1255516_comment'></div>因有媒孽其短者，谓公以廉自喜，而中书有成规之言，盖嫁怨焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_380_1255516_comment'></div>自是求瑕甚悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_381_1255516_comment'></div>一日过州，得二事，锐意欲按治，以委晋陵宰李璹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_382_1255516_comment'></div>璹力言其无有，曰：「兹事如有之，安能掩众人耳目？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_383_1255516_comment'></div>且监司有所劾，必合公论，乃终无悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_384_1255516_comment'></div>彼人皆曰贤而害之，无终悔乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_385_1255516_comment'></div>漕大愧，引道去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_386_1255516_comment'></div>于是属吏之干荐者，胥吏之惧罪者，多受风旨，至讽寓居过客以求公短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_387_1255516_comment'></div>自春迄冬，了不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_388_1255516_comment'></div>岁莫再道旧治，惭前事不效，毛举数事以劾，皆公事，又无其实，坐是罢郡，远近冤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_389_1255516_comment'></div>自漕之相伺察也，人人危之，公初不为动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_390_1255516_comment'></div>或劝引避者，曰：「吾内省不疚，以朝命典此州，俟谴黜尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_391_1255516_comment'></div>虽漕吏亦以此服公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_392_1255516_comment'></div>及罢归，未尝片辞自辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_393_1255516_comment'></div>有言及漕，如未尝相失，虽家人父子间，不见其有忿色也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_394_1255516_comment'></div>自是，凡三领崇道祠事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_395_1255516_comment'></div>公自罢郡，买田筑室，慨然有终焉志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_396_1255516_comment'></div>公所居占水竹之胜，幅巾杖屦，与邻里相往来，否则閒居一室，左右图史，视一世荣利泊如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_397_1255516_comment'></div>如是者十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_398_1255516_comment'></div>故人给事中刘公一止来见公，喜曰：「公形癯而神昌，养之如此，岂古所谓得道者耶」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_399_1255516_comment'></div>既而得微疾，以绍兴二十有七年二月十有三日薨，享年六十有七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_400_1255516_comment'></div>官累右中散大夫，以久次赐服金紫，开国馀杭县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_401_1255516_comment'></div>公资禀既异，涵养有道，内外修整，色夷气清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_402_1255516_comment'></div>嗜读书，博览强记，自少迨老，手抄口诵，未尝释卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_403_1255516_comment'></div>前言往行，往往成诵，取其要领以修身行己，期于有用，非特玩其文章而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_404_1255516_comment'></div>人以疑事疑义质诸公，一言立决，问者冰释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_405_1255516_comment'></div>为文敏捷立成，尤积思于诗，以诗名世者，皆见推许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_406_1255516_comment'></div>公尝语人曰：「吾不事场屋，不干举荐，未尝为外所挫，故吾之乐也全」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_407_1255516_comment'></div>平生以清约为尚，无所嗜好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_408_1255516_comment'></div>自少年以来，未尝历媱坊酒肆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_409_1255516_comment'></div>若夫纷华盛丽，性所不悦，非勉强而去之者，人以为公有外曾祖父赵清献公之风也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_410_1255516_comment'></div>仁而爱物，内刚明而外和易，后己而先人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_411_1255516_comment'></div>少壮时敏而锐，勇于立事，居正而行，自谓贲育莫能夺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_412_1255516_comment'></div>晚节益以盛德服人，杜门却扫，宅心物表，渊然其静，泰然其安，对之使人不善之心销也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_413_1255516_comment'></div>早从学浮屠者游，出语简妙，多得其指归，临终神色不乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_414_1255516_comment'></div>善与人交，久而不渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_415_1255516_comment'></div>明而善容物，未尝恶于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_416_1255516_comment'></div>世人嗜好相反，有若荼荠，及语公，皆心服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_417_1255516_comment'></div>盖其处心平恕、待人如一而然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_418_1255516_comment'></div>闻人之善，欣然如出诸己，虽异己者犹喜道之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_419_1255516_comment'></div>街谈巷议有可取者，不废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_420_1255516_comment'></div>既老，以「乐闻过」名其斋，且自述其意，为文置左右，闻者益服其进德云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_421_1255516_comment'></div>于内外姻戚，曲尽恩意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_422_1255516_comment'></div>少尝与季父架阁公献明同居，开府公殁，架阁公养生送死甚力，既而亦下世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_423_1255516_comment'></div>公经理其家，始终不怠，士夫谈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_424_1255516_comment'></div>族人之无归者，尤悉意存抚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_425_1255516_comment'></div>其任子也，舍其孙而官其从父兄弟之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_426_1255516_comment'></div>既属纩，舌本强不能掉，家人环问所欲言，但能道孤侄女名字而已，闻者泣下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_427_1255516_comment'></div>既殁，虽庸夫贱隶无不涕洟咨嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_428_1255516_comment'></div>公行己于其细者，每所加意，盖不胜载，而大节著于宣州城守时，故某纪之特详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_429_1255516_comment'></div>宣人周右司紫芝尝为某言：「当寇迫时，一日见公圃亭，忽睇视自语曰：『何期今日乃死于此』？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_430_1255516_comment'></div>方食，意不在匕箸也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_431_1255516_comment'></div>以此观之，初未尝有去志，非侥倖得名者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_432_1255516_comment'></div>周每言之，心形俱服云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_433_1255516_comment'></div>公娶同郡元氏，直龙图阁积中曾孙女，封令人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_434_1255516_comment'></div>生二男一女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_435_1255516_comment'></div>长男曰系，将仕郎，未冠而夭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_436_1255516_comment'></div>幼曰修年，以公任从事郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_437_1255516_comment'></div>女嫁右宣义郎曾某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_438_1255516_comment'></div>孙男女三人：男曰回，并幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_439_1255516_comment'></div>其孤某以二十有七年四月十有四日葬公于临安府钱塘县履泰乡郁家山之原，实迩开府公墓，从公志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_440_1255516_comment'></div>唯公于圹宜有铭，于国史宜有传，于墓隧宜有碑，谨掇公言行，以告世之立言者，求铭而刻诸幽，且备异日史官采择云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_441_1255516_comment'></div>某月日，右宣义郎、知湖州长兴县丞、主管学事曾某状。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_442_1255516'></div><div id='poem_sentence_442_1255516_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　任满，有求批书启。作品：《长兴丞任满求批书启》<div id='poem_1255485' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255485' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255485?labeling=true' target='_blank'>长兴丞任满求批书启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255485")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255485_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255485'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255485'>课难自脱，当谨俟于谴诃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255485_comment'></div>情或可哀，敢尽输于悃愊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255485_comment'></div>遂忘僭冒，辄叩高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255485_comment'></div>窃念某樗栎散材，草茅下品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255485_comment'></div>早失庭趋之训，粗窥家有之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255485_comment'></div>叨世赏以得官，慨先声之坠地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255485_comment'></div>碌碌尘埃之末，区区簿领之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255485_comment'></div>策蹇磨铅，冀逃瘝旷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255485_comment'></div>饮冰食蘖，祈免悔尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255485_comment'></div>既择地以不详，每吁天而奚及？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255485_comment'></div>载念幅员之内，率遵什一之供。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255485_comment'></div>食租衣税者既非妄输，凿井耕田者岂容苟免？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255485_comment'></div>虽曰徵科之有限，其如剧易之不同！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255485_comment'></div>维是长城，素名大邑，赋繁俗犷，地瘠人贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255485_comment'></div>武断乡曲者履犴狱如夷涂，家无见粮者视铢两为奇货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255485_comment'></div>顽悍或难移于岁月，饥寒或莫保于朝昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255485_comment'></div>兼二者之至难，视一州而特异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255485_comment'></div>适此及瓜之代，尚遥登谷之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255485_comment'></div>阅时已迫于常期，问数始盈于大半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255485_comment'></div>自占阳城之考，诚所甘心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255485_comment'></div>却回墨翟之车，固知无益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255485_comment'></div>风中鹢退，不许过都；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255485_comment'></div>纸尾雁行，复难占位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255485_comment'></div>第徬徨而无措，姑黾勉以自宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255485_comment'></div>解印绶以径行，于今不可；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255485_comment'></div>挂衣冠而长往，其决已难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255485_comment'></div>一从袖手以傍观，始悔噬脐之何及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255485_comment'></div>方州郡交嗤其不职，而士民或悯其复来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255485_comment'></div>虽不能如古人之为，课吏以最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255485_comment'></div>然告之以使君之怒，言或见从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255485_comment'></div>顾何力之有焉，多相踵而来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255485_comment'></div>方令行郡境，敢代帅以受名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1255485_comment'></div>且政出县官，真因人而成事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1255485_comment'></div>正谋身之无策，敢藉手以陈辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1255485_comment'></div>念大贤何所不容，自知获免；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1255485_comment'></div>若小人必文其过，终不忍为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1255485_comment'></div>恭惟枢密相公寰宇真贤，岩廊旧德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1255485_comment'></div>举正己之事以正物，推爱君之心而爱民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1255485_comment'></div>清约出于天资，安静符于人欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1255485_comment'></div>政声四达，治状上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1255485_comment'></div>扶杖叩阍，恐此日君侯之去；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1255485_comment'></div>赐书增秩，慰一方父老之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1255485_comment'></div>姑从河内之留，来即颍川之拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1255485_comment'></div>宽和服物，尝表见于赞书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1255485_comment'></div>轻约待人，岂犹遗于下品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1255485_comment'></div>敢陈始末，幸辱哀怜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1255485_comment'></div>某傥以馀庥，尚尘仕路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1255485_comment'></div>铭心异日，齰舌前非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1255485_comment'></div>谨期会以为先，敢许知事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1255485_comment'></div>罄夙宵而自勉，庶补将来。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1255485_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
嵊州（嵊县）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3479ad79476c45bd8e8a9d35df8e2b22_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3479ad79476c45bd8e8a9d35df8e2b22");'><span id='3479ad79476c45bd8e8a9d35df8e2b22_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1159')">1158-1159年</a>，40-41岁</div><div id='3479ad79476c45bd8e8a9d35df8e2b22' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　为嵊县丞。有通太守启。作品：《嵊县丞通太守启》<div id='poem_1255486' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255486' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255486?labeling=true' target='_blank'>嵊县丞通太守启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255486")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255486_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255486'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255486'>得调铨曹，效官岩邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255486_comment'></div>既获居于封部，将仰奉于条章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255486_comment'></div>引脰知归，扪心自幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255486_comment'></div>恭惟某官斯民先觉，间世伟材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255486_comment'></div>孕天地之元精，际风云之盛会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255486_comment'></div>身兼数器之美，气备四时之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255486_comment'></div>国有蓍龟，卓矣典刑之旧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255486_comment'></div>人瞻斗岳，巍然德义之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255486_comment'></div>自奉对于大廷，早结知于黈纩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255486_comment'></div>久负经纶之业，暂烦镇抚之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255486_comment'></div>立玉英姿，自与山川而映发；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255486_comment'></div>摛云大手，坐令草木以增华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255486_comment'></div>兵卫森罗，节旄交峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255486_comment'></div>拥六州之鼓吹，控百越之江山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255486_comment'></div>棋布列城，安教条之不扰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255486_comment'></div>云屯万旅，谨号令以无哗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255486_comment'></div>聊嬉老监之镜湖，合傍玉皇之香案。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255486_comment'></div>裤襦何慕，共推仁者之安仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255486_comment'></div>衮绣以归，自是相门之出相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255486_comment'></div>某琐庸无取，历落多奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255486_comment'></div>早窥家有之书，莫逮庭趋之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255486_comment'></div>腼颜场屋，已坠世科；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255486_comment'></div>俯首簿书，尚尘官使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255486_comment'></div>低徊十载，黾勉半生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255486_comment'></div>第属吏之贪廉，傥占真清之目；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255486_comment'></div>覈下官之勤惰，敢贻涉笔之讥？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255486_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1255486_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年2月14日</a>　王纶自工部侍郎兼直学士院除同知枢密院事，上启致贺。作品：《贺王同知启》<div id='poem_1255476' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255476' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255476?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺王同知启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年2月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255476")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255476_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255476'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255476'>窃审进从鳌禁，入秉鸿枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255476_comment'></div>风烈所加，未见真儒之敌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255476_comment'></div>仪型自远，共知有德之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255476_comment'></div>恭惟某官识际天人，学该今古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255476_comment'></div>持赤心而致主，蕴素业以经邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255476_comment'></div>全器难名，文武维其所用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255476_comment'></div>精忠不挠，安危任之以身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255476_comment'></div>高怀不改于险夷，浩气兼全于刚大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255476_comment'></div>久持笔橐，独结冕旒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255476_comment'></div>辩贯六经，聊探立谈之白璧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255476_comment'></div>文成数刻，曾倾买赋之黄金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255476_comment'></div>自闻盛事之传，共企徽章之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255476_comment'></div>延邹、枚之客右，久受圣知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255476_comment'></div>得颇、牧于禁中，更膺天奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255476_comment'></div>且熙代历推于庶姓，维相门特盛于诸王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255476_comment'></div>匪惟冠冕之相望，抑亦简编之有纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255476_comment'></div>或谋谟德业，凛然有大臣之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255476_comment'></div>或学问文章，卓尔为百世之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255476_comment'></div>适临昌运，更出伟人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255476_comment'></div>方当图任之初，允属迩遐之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255476_comment'></div>某早窥声采，尝辱甄披。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255476_comment'></div>狐腋虽多，未弃一毛之陋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255476_comment'></div>骥足可附，不难千里之遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255476_comment'></div>方自托于陶镕，曾不知其鼓舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255476_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1255476_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年闰6月</a>　周麟之除翰林学士，上启致贺。作品：《贺周内翰茂振启》<div id='poem_1255479' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255479' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255479?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺周内翰茂振启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年闰6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255479")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255479_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255479'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255479'>伏审诏发中宸，朝登内相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255479_comment'></div>极盛世文儒之选，冠清朝供奉之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255479_comment'></div>方满岁为真，固四海倾心之已久；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255479_comment'></div>而旧人共政，岂九重注意之自今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255479_comment'></div>窃以历代以来，百官备设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255479_comment'></div>翰墨文章之任，自昔尤难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255479_comment'></div>论思献纳之流，于斯为最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255479_comment'></div>自从臣列于盛汉，成中外义理之文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255479_comment'></div>暨学士置于有唐，居台省司存之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255479_comment'></div>官尊禄厚，地秘职亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255479_comment'></div>自非声华高出于具僚，体裁遍周于众制，其辞章渊蕴大而为郊天告庙之文，而藻绘绪馀小可及警夜眠儿之作，赏善罚恶劝惩于百辟，发号施令鼓舞于四方，岂惟密赞于圣谟，抑亦显裨于治效，宁令虚位，必待真材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255479_comment'></div>第惊宠数之甚优，可见倚毗之甚重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255479_comment'></div>调和给君羹之美，辉光分宫烛之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255479_comment'></div>紫禁相连，自远人间之风日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255479_comment'></div>金阶不远，可攀天上之星辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255479_comment'></div>振古以还，得人而重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255479_comment'></div>恭惟某官英风盖世，间气自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255479_comment'></div>高文追三代之醇，嘉论合六经之正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255479_comment'></div>连鸧叠中，颇弯弓盘马之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255479_comment'></div>一鹗孤骞，骋耸壑昂霄之便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255479_comment'></div>嘉猷辰告，令闻日彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255479_comment'></div>西掖东台，遍仪要近；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255479_comment'></div>南官北户，历践清华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255479_comment'></div>尚稽图任之崇，共识登庸之渐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255479_comment'></div>江山环绕，助开胸次之奇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255479_comment'></div>雨露鼎来，输作笔端之润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255479_comment'></div>暂直复门之邃，径跻二府之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255479_comment'></div>设绝礼于坐中，巃光可待；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255479_comment'></div>绕曼声于殿上，显册将颁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255479_comment'></div>某早以孱庸，误蒙甄录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255479_comment'></div>施大恩于卵翼，借馀论于齿牙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255479_comment'></div>有愧诗人，身伴凝严之直；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1255479_comment'></div>方同武将，涕流宽大之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1255479_comment'></div>益殚依斗之心，愿毕在镕之赐<span class='inlineComment2'>（《云庄集》卷三。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1255479_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1255479'>第：原无，据四库本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1255479_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年9月14日</a>　汤思退拜左仆射，又上启致贺。作品：《贺汤相再除左揆启》<div id='poem_1255470' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255470' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255470?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺汤相再除左揆启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年9月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255470")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255470_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255470'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255470'>敬审诞告明廷，延登元宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255470_comment'></div>代天理物，时居百揆之先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255470_comment'></div>开国承家，仍越五侯之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255470_comment'></div>锡宠名而由旧，兼命数以惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255470_comment'></div>礼绝群工，庆均四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255470_comment'></div>生灵鼓舞，宗社奠安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255470_comment'></div>窃以左右之置傅岩，虽均作相之任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255470_comment'></div>一二以资仲父，当极为臣之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255470_comment'></div>要令首出于百僚，斯可下宜于万物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255470_comment'></div>精神相得，亶称千载之亲逢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255470_comment'></div>位貌绝殊，将使万邦之为宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255470_comment'></div>推一心而无间，展四体以不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255470_comment'></div>志合道同，将见得君之专也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255470_comment'></div>官尊职大，盖将举国而听焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255470_comment'></div>恭惟某官道际天人，名高夷夏，得圣人耦，应三聘以幡然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255470_comment'></div>为帝者师，出一编而足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255470_comment'></div>著外抚内亲之效，彰出藩入辅之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255470_comment'></div>会圣皇遵汾水之游，命旧德起平泉之佚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255470_comment'></div>无烦肖象，具存《说命》之三篇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255470_comment'></div>不待割烹，咸识伊躬之五就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255470_comment'></div>际遗大投艰之运，开重熙累洽之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255470_comment'></div>方将建一柱以扶明堂，示六符以昭上彖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255470_comment'></div>合谋猷为黼扆，共图万世之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255470_comment'></div>收威柄于庙堂，坐制四方之动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255470_comment'></div>果闻作命，重冠在庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255470_comment'></div>山川土田，大启周公之宇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255470_comment'></div>衮冕黻廷，益隆汉相之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255470_comment'></div>伟东第之复开，极人间之至乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255470_comment'></div>䌽衣入谢，再观上相之进趋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255470_comment'></div>象服受仪，四展回班之庆贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255470_comment'></div>耸高风于绅笏，流盛事于简编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255470_comment'></div>助圣朝孝治之风，为天下人子之劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1255470_comment'></div>岂止二十四考，阅岁时礼貌之加；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1255470_comment'></div>盖将万有千年，观朝夕精神之聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1255470_comment'></div>极幅舄带裳之盛，增旂常鼎鼐之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1255470_comment'></div>某井谷寒生，门阑旧物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1255470_comment'></div>自惟朴樕，早出炉锤，每怜朽质之穷，益甚曲成之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1255470_comment'></div>舞手蹈足，莫殚欣喜之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1255470_comment'></div>附翼攀鳞，期赴功名之会。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1255470_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年12月21日</a>　王纶除知枢密院事，再上启致贺。作品：《贺王知院启》<div id='poem_1255474' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255474' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255474?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺王知院启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年12月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255474")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255474_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255474'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255474'>窃审诞敷诏綍，登冠枢庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255474_comment'></div>帷幄居中，密运止戈之武；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255474_comment'></div>陛廉增峻，益隆助德之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255474_comment'></div>历考简编，灼见古昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255474_comment'></div>三监甫定，周爰作于六师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255474_comment'></div>百粤既平，汉始增于七校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255474_comment'></div>盖欲示威于无敌，亦将备患于未萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255474_comment'></div>凡遇昌期，必张武备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255474_comment'></div>连营置将，责以训齐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255474_comment'></div>无事养兵，贵于整暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255474_comment'></div>既用命无设施之所，而均劳以安靖之常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255474_comment'></div>甘苦绝异而上下之情寖疏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255474_comment'></div>宴安可怀，而纪律之防易弛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255474_comment'></div>必有志术，得其忠心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255474_comment'></div>使之饱暖逸居，常若衔恩之未报；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255474_comment'></div>必也威爱允济，乃或流涕而用刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255474_comment'></div>结之也浃肌肤之深，驭之也如臂指之易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255474_comment'></div>心悦诚服，怀平日之拊循；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255474_comment'></div>命贱威尊，待一朝之号令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255474_comment'></div>虽赴汤蹈火而可用，况按甲休徒之匪艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255474_comment'></div>助成万世之安，坐却四方之侮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255474_comment'></div>凡兹军政之可纪，实自庙谟之有人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255474_comment'></div>维是杰材，独膺重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255474_comment'></div>恭惟某官材兼文武，名盖华夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255474_comment'></div>劲气精忠，干云霄而直上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255474_comment'></div>正言谠论，质鬼神而不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255474_comment'></div>自许以古人之为，可任以天下之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255474_comment'></div>昔居乌府，多胆落于霜威；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255474_comment'></div>寖陟銮坡，亦涕流于云诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255474_comment'></div>已知诸将之尽服，犹俟三年之有成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255474_comment'></div>自升枢斗之崇，果阅星霜之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255474_comment'></div>折冲绥远，爰酬命数之新；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1255474_comment'></div>经体赞元，行副登庸之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1255474_comment'></div>某久厕曳裾之列，尝叨赠衮之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1255474_comment'></div>仰之弥高，同有具瞻之志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1255474_comment'></div>喜而不寐，独怀起舞之心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1255474_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年12月</a>　作有《大愚堂记》<div id='poem_1255509' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255509' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255509?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大愚堂记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十九年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255509")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255509_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255509'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255509'>子章子启山林于具区之上，环亘百亩，亭观相临，径术相错。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255509_comment'></div>仰有苍翠，俯有清泚，四时草木，行布而族别，夸奇而竞秀，升高视下，闻见层出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255509_comment'></div>章子乐之，益种秫以备酒材，畜鱼以供膳羞，果蔬薪樵取足于畛域之内，而择其地之中结庐以为家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255509_comment'></div>朝于是，夕于是，宴然不知岁月之迁流而外物之可羡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255509_comment'></div>乃名其堂曰「大愚」，而谓客曰：「吾闻古之愚者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255509_comment'></div>坐进此道，终日不违者，有如颜渊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255509_comment'></div>卷舒无方，知不能及者，有如宁武子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255509_comment'></div>是皆抱贤人之资，以愚自托者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255509_comment'></div>我则异于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255509_comment'></div>其行于于，其处籧籧，不知功业之可慕与爵禄之可趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255509_comment'></div>得丧交于前而无所择，事物接于心而无所居，盖天下之真愚者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255509_comment'></div>今吾筑圃以自休，揭之居室以沐浴于斯言，其可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255509_comment'></div>客曰：「有是哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255509_comment'></div>夫子之能名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255509_comment'></div>吾悲夫智之为累也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255509_comment'></div>夫人之生，四支百体，筋骨绵络，至弱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255509_comment'></div>利害诱于外，思虑动于内，物交于物，日自戕贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255509_comment'></div>甚矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255509_comment'></div>智之害吾身也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255509_comment'></div>天地之间，人物错居，而惟机心之为胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255509_comment'></div>人伪兴而天真远，剽攘争夺将无不为也，罟获陷阱将无不至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255509_comment'></div>智者满于天下，而天下之人始踧踖而不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255509_comment'></div>甚矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255509_comment'></div>智之害天下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255509_comment'></div>其于己也，所得不足以补所失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255509_comment'></div>其于人也，所利不足以偿所害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255509_comment'></div>夫子知其然，望其末流而塞其源，息迹灭影，以愚自全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255509_comment'></div>此老氏所谓盛德，而仲尼独以回也为贤者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255509_comment'></div>虽然，愚而为诈，愚而好自用，愚而不及于中，固非夫子之所病也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255509_comment'></div>若夫坐于堂上，离形去知，堕支体，黜聪明，恝然游于物之初，则彼所谓智者固不得而累我矣，而此所谓愚者，亦安得而名之耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255509_comment'></div>章子掀髯，一笑而作，客因书以为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255509_comment'></div>绍兴己卯十二月戊戌，南丰曾某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1255509_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
镇江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0c6bd9b4346142efba1a20e0eff22c19_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0c6bd9b4346142efba1a20e0eff22c19");'><span id='0c6bd9b4346142efba1a20e0eff22c19_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1163')">1160-1163年</a>，42-45岁</div><div id='0c6bd9b4346142efba1a20e0eff22c19' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　监镇江诸军司粮料院。到任，有谢启。作品：《行在诸军司粮料院谢启》<div id='poem_1255489' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255489' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255489?labeling=true' target='_blank'>行在诸军粮料院谢启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255489")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255489_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255489'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255489'>已试罔功，宜在黜幽之典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255489_comment'></div>惟新作命，更谐重内之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255489_comment'></div>腼面知惭，抚躬无措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255489_comment'></div>窃以以禄驭富，示至尊操柄之专；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255489_comment'></div>聚人曰财，致群下干城之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255489_comment'></div>凡隶名于军籍，率仰给于县官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255489_comment'></div>列栅绮分，伍符山积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255489_comment'></div>科级既非一致，等威几至万殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255489_comment'></div>人事所难，擐甲兵而即死；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255489_comment'></div>主恩欲报，援枹鼓以忘身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255489_comment'></div>使之盈志气于无事之时，所以责勇敢于有为之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255489_comment'></div>刻肌铭骨，莫移平日之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255489_comment'></div>糜首捐躯，期效一朝之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255489_comment'></div>阚若虎貔之勇，浩乎鹅鹳之繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255489_comment'></div>或始委质以从戎，或既策功而赐爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255489_comment'></div>不可以人而悦，使赋予之有遍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255489_comment'></div>则惟计铢而称，在均平而不失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255489_comment'></div>当求开敏，以济事功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255489_comment'></div>如某者井谷寒乡，簪緌遗绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255489_comment'></div>未替诗书之习，尚馀孝谨之承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255489_comment'></div>粤自高曾以来，不以父兄而进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255489_comment'></div>家繇儒显，传四代之文科；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255489_comment'></div>世以直闻，受七朝之眷奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255489_comment'></div>藐兹小子，愧我先人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255489_comment'></div>伤辞气之两衰，抚懦愚而何用！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255489_comment'></div>家徒四壁，莫专探讨之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255489_comment'></div>智效一官，不救啼号之迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255489_comment'></div>顷从疏贱，初被使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255489_comment'></div>蔑闻横草之功，俄请及瓜之代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255489_comment'></div>名无赫赫，惭非何武之居官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255489_comment'></div>言本平平，惧向班生而问策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255489_comment'></div>既趣装于官次，方结绶于王畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1255489_comment'></div>夫何顽钝之姿，遽受生成之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1255489_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇某官<span class='inlineComment2'>（入颂德云云。）</span>某敢不䌷绎旧闻，激昂懦质？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1255489_comment'></div>会计当而已，宁怀下位之惭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1255489_comment'></div>诵说云乎哉，益励北行之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1255489_comment'></div>庶收薄效，上答殊私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1255489_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_1255489'></div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1255489_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　监镇江诸军司粮料院。与王质、李处全聚首，有序送王质。作品：《送王景文教授归江西序》<div id='poem_1255502' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255502' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255502?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送王景文教授归江西序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255502")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255502_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255502'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255502'>某族子熹，颇有大志，喜交天下奇伟士，尝为余道郭从范、王景文、李粹伯之为人，虽未识面，常往来余怀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255502_comment'></div>前年客郭城，始得从范稠人中，往来日相亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255502_comment'></div>一日过族子家，而景文适至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255502_comment'></div>是年冬，官京口，则粹伯又先在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255502_comment'></div>盖向所慕爱者，一旦尽得之为交游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255502_comment'></div>今年从范无禄早世，而粹伯、景文始同擢第以归，徘徊于大江之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255502_comment'></div>二公骤相过，某也幸辄介处其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255502_comment'></div>记景文初相遇时微有酒，所议论逸发，粲然成文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255502_comment'></div>迈往之气，郁郁出眉宇间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255502_comment'></div>某于是知族子之言不吾欺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255502_comment'></div>当是时，景文名满天下，要官大人，犹忘势愿交，而某迫行役不暇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255502_comment'></div>今幸相遇于此，暑风凉日，举杯以相属，登高临深，摄衣以相从，岂非天耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255502_comment'></div>每念取友之难，而会合之不易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255502_comment'></div>闻其来，辄挽不听去；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255502_comment'></div>属其谈，惟恐止也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255502_comment'></div>又时为某出诗骚、古文，虽体裁之不齐，而位置施设，各当机杼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255502_comment'></div>每愧叹弥日，始知曩时得景文，犹有所未尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255502_comment'></div>尝与之上危亭，抚江山，豁然以惊，怡然而嬉，曰：「天下壮观，尽在是矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255502_comment'></div>酒酣起舞，回立四顾，则又悠然以思，愀然以悲，曰：「古今一山川也，曩之陈迹了然在吾目中，而其人不可得而见」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255502_comment'></div>景文者，岂若夫骚人墨客悲伤憔悴而为是言也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255502_comment'></div>景文胸怀朗朗，疏眉而哆口，欣然有大夫之表，腹如盘而背若负也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255502_comment'></div>然则其任大也固宜，景文勉之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255502_comment'></div>气之养也愈深，则其发也愈奇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255502_comment'></div>术之择也愈审，则其用也愈精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255502_comment'></div>使后之人登斯亭，览故迹，抗怀遐想，知千载之上有王景文者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255502_comment'></div>书竹帛而上鼎钟，慨然有不同时之叹者，必自今日始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255502_comment'></div>而某则亲周旋其间，又自知幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255502_comment'></div>是为序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1255502_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　在镇江与王质、李处全唱和。作品：《李粹伯对月见怀次韵》《夜饮枕流次日以诗记陈迹》《再饮枕流和王景文韵》《李粹伯命赋枕流已读佳篇不容着语戏书二伽陀问之》《点绛唇•送李粹伯赴春闱》<div id='poem_220045' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_220045' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/220045?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李粹伯对月见怀次韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_220045_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_220045'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_220045'>初收雨脚万丝悬，妙手谁人补漏天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_220045_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_220045'>佳月素华迷夜旦，好诗馀味满中边<span class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_219990'>淅淅好风天似水，纷纷高论气如虹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_219990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_219990'>罚筹猬起觞无算，醉骨山颓榼屡空。<div id='poem_sentence_0_220081'>小驻征骖，一尊古寺留君住。<div id='poem_sentence_0_220081_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_220081'>六花无数。<div id='poem_sentence_1_220081_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_220081'>飞舞朝天路。<div id='poem_sentence_2_220081_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_220081'>上苑繁华，却似词章富。<div id='poem_sentence_3_220081_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_220081'>春将暮。<div id='poem_sentence_4_220081_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_220081'>玉鞭凝伫。<div id='poem_sentence_5_220081_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_220081'>总是经行处。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_220081_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　镇江任满，通交代龚判院启。作品：《镇江任满通交代龚判院启》<div id='poem_1255488' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255488' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255488?labeling=true' target='_blank'>镇江任满通交代龚判院启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255488")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255488_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255488'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255488'>乡风南北，居多景慕之私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255488_comment'></div>随牒后先，偶有交承之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255488_comment'></div>事逾愿始，喜溢颜间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255488_comment'></div>恭惟某官议论纵横，辞情慷慨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255488_comment'></div>学穷渊奥，伟家法之得传；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255488_comment'></div>气禀浑全，凛祖风之不坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255488_comment'></div>久宜阔步，适尔假涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255488_comment'></div>均常数于廪庖，岂劳施设？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255488_comment'></div>沸欢声于将士，聊助威灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255488_comment'></div>行观凤诏之华，入簉鹓行之邃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255488_comment'></div>某孤踪连蹇，弱质伶俜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255488_comment'></div>缅怀先祖之在朝，实与大贤而汇进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255488_comment'></div>自微而显，三腾论荐之章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255488_comment'></div>以退为高，一上晚留之奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255488_comment'></div>虽裔子贤愚之绝异，而两家臭味之固同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255488_comment'></div>曾是孱庸，更深契好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255488_comment'></div>并英游于此日，已怀扬秕之惭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255488_comment'></div>仰荣路于他年，敢起积薪之叹！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255488_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1255488_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年1月</a>　闲居镇江，有上时相书。作品：《辛巳上时相书》<div id='poem_1255495' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255495' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255495?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辛巳上时相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255495")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255495_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255495'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255495'>正月某日，右宣教郎、前监分差镇江府诸军司粮料院曾某，谨斋沐裁书，百拜献于平章仆射相公阁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255495_comment'></div>某闻进言之难，自古然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255495_comment'></div>高之则张皇而不可通，卑之则会粹而不足取，是言之果无益于干人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255495_comment'></div>鬷蔑一言而得之于堂下，阮瞻三语而置之于幕府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255495_comment'></div>名位之相辽，贵贱之相求，言之不可以已也如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255495_comment'></div>虽然，言之之难，莫难于今之朝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255495_comment'></div>非为忌讳壅敝而不欲闻也，非有声音颜色之拒人也，而其所以难者何故？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255495_comment'></div>特以海内乂安，朝廷清明，百官承序，盗贼屏迹，又何用哓哓然多言为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255495_comment'></div>某闻三代之盛时莫如成周，而周公之诗曰：「迨天之未阴雨，彻彼桑士，绸缪牖户」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255495_comment'></div>方是时，囹圄空虚者四十馀年，越裳氏重九译而至，制礼作乐以文太平之时也，何阴雨之足戒？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255495_comment'></div>何牖户之当谨耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255495_comment'></div>此盖圣人当极治之时，耻一事之不举，于持盈之际，为万世之远图，长虑却顾，殆过于抢攘纷纭之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255495_comment'></div>某窃料阁下以周公之心为心，而某愿有言焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255495_comment'></div>今事之大者，不可以讼言，而其可言者有四：一曰正风俗，二曰重命令，三曰择计臣，四曰戒狱吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255495_comment'></div>某闻今世之患，悉在于民志之不定，自舆台以上皆有侈心，此最有国之大患也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255495_comment'></div>古之圣人谨上下之分，宫室有制，舆马有度，衣服有章，器用有等，人徒有数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255495_comment'></div>凡为此者，岂夺民之所愿而强其所恶者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255495_comment'></div>诚以为物之生有限，而人之欲无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255495_comment'></div>以有限之生而给无穷之欲，安得而不屈？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255495_comment'></div>是故汲汲于明分者，无他，将以兼足天下而已耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255495_comment'></div>《易》曰：「辨上下，定民志」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255495_comment'></div>夫民志之不定，自常人视之，如不甚急；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255495_comment'></div>而圣人深忧之，丁宁著之于经，以谓民志定则上下辨，上下辨则财力有馀，而天下不臻于富足者，未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255495_comment'></div>古者五十而后食肉，七十而后衣帛，今也自童稚时晏然家居而享侯伯之奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255495_comment'></div>闾阎之人，绮襦玉食，竞为侈靡，嫁娶丧葬，率踰礼制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255495_comment'></div>力有不足，则疾视其胜己者，而求其财力之有馀，盗窃之不作，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255495_comment'></div>或者乃以是为迂阔之论，呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255495_comment'></div>世之所以望于阁下者，岂为区区钱谷甲兵之间哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255495_comment'></div>今主上克己自励，躬尚冲素，以风天下，不为不至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255495_comment'></div>愿公卿大臣奉明天子之德意，而倡率之于下，毅然力行，以示四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255495_comment'></div>庶几风俗一变，家给人足，太平之极，功无大于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255495_comment'></div>某之所谓正风俗者此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1255495_comment'></div>某闻亏令者诛，益令者诛，不行令者诛，留令者诛，不从令者诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1255495_comment'></div>令之下如涣汗，如流水，如雷之不一，如风之不再。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1255495_comment'></div>夫惟不出，出之必行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1255495_comment'></div>夫惟不发，发之必达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1255495_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1255495_comment'></div>其虑之也审，则其从之也易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1255495_comment'></div>其事当于人心，则人皆鼓舞而趋向之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1255495_comment'></div>今也朝廷急于求言，从之如转圜，盖千载一时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1255495_comment'></div>而人之智虑未必皆精，议论未必皆当，悉举而行，殆无遗者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1255495_comment'></div>然是之于前或非之于后，从之于暂或革之于久，或未见其利而已受其害，或得其一而不得其二，郡县格而弗行，吏胥舞而为奸，遂与良法美意、德音明诏并为文具，无祗恪奉行之意，良可惜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1255495_comment'></div>国家法令明具，所患者不能推行之耳，固不在于纷纷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1255495_comment'></div>某愿一令之出，反复熟议，极其利害而后行，毋轻出令，而郡县之吏毋擅沮令，毋辄议令，如此则下知所从，而上之作命不为虚文矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1255495_comment'></div>某之所谓重命令者，此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1255495_comment'></div>某闻《易》曰：「何以守位？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1255495_comment'></div>曰仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1255495_comment'></div>何以聚人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1255495_comment'></div>曰财」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1255495_comment'></div>故财计者，有国之最急，而令之所宜先也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1255495_comment'></div>仓廪既实，府库既充，可以固根本，可以施惠泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1255495_comment'></div>静而守成，则可以修礼文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1255495_comment'></div>动而守成，则可以抗威武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1255495_comment'></div>惟所欲之，无不如志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1255495_comment'></div>国家政本惠养，变政易令，归于裕民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1255495_comment'></div>每下蠲复之诏，尽罢无名之献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1255495_comment'></div>为移东就西之说者，无有也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1255495_comment'></div>陈损下益上之术者，无有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1255495_comment'></div>美则美矣，然矫枉者或过其正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1255495_comment'></div>商功计利之臣，人耻名之，理财之事几至于不讲，左支右吾，玩岁愒日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1255495_comment'></div>圣上时出内帑以佐国计，甚德盛也，然非经国之远图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1255495_comment'></div>数年以来，掌计之臣，更出迭入，席未煖而辄去，算计见效，何以得也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1255495_comment'></div>故责成莫如久任，久任莫如慎择，规模先定，按图而求之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1255495_comment'></div>不知今日金钱粟帛所从入者岁凡几何，廪给之度赐予之节，岁又几何，其盈虚之数凡几何，为水旱之备者又几何，前人之所谓《会计录》者尝有之欤，某不得而知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1255495_comment'></div>若或未然，愿阁下少留意焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1255495_comment'></div>择之慎，用之久，毋苟岁月，毋怀顾望，则一登再登三登之数，当见于今者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1255495_comment'></div>某之所谓择计臣者，此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1255495_comment'></div>某闻刑者，侀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1255495_comment'></div>侀者，成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1255495_comment'></div>一成而不可变，故君子尽心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1255495_comment'></div>刑辟之设，圣人禁暴止奸不得已而为之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1255495_comment'></div>故曰：「如得其情，则哀矜而勿喜」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1255495_comment'></div>夫欲得其情，五听之所及，三刺之所加，如斯而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1255495_comment'></div>不幸而索罪于箠楚之下，固已远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1255495_comment'></div>桁杨刀锯陈于前，徽纆梏拲列于后，而人始无所措其手足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1255495_comment'></div>至或巧为鞫囚之具，惨毒万状，见之者胆落，闻之者心悸，甚非圣世之所宜有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1255495_comment'></div>使所治者皆奸猾巨蠹，何为而不可？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1255495_comment'></div>至于情伪未分，迹状未具，将于此乎求之，孰谓内无善良懦弱之人，而畏威诬服者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1255495_comment'></div>使狱吏善听耶，舍此亦可以得之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1255495_comment'></div>如其不然，其滥及善人也多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1255495_comment'></div>当戒者未戒，可毁者未毁，伤败和气，莫此为甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1255495_comment'></div>孟子曰：「国家閒暇，明其政刑」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1255495_comment'></div>此正无事之时，所宜深思而痛革之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1255495_comment'></div>某之所谓当戒狱吏者，此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1255495_comment'></div>凡某之所言，朝廷之上已讲究而施行之，则某为喋喋矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1255495_comment'></div>不然，则千虑一得，不为无分毫补也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1255495_comment'></div>某不佞，生于宗绪颓落之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1255495_comment'></div>自束发以来，妄以振起为任，诵古今，考成败，不可谓无其志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1255495_comment'></div>少蒙尊亲之教育，长闻师友之议论，亦不为不多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1255495_comment'></div>而资本顽顿，迄不能自致于名流，宦游踰三十年，困踬朱墨间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1255495_comment'></div>昨者受代造朝，适阁下参大政，始得登门阑，聆謦欬，望颜色，忘其疏贱，以书干下执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1255495_comment'></div>首蒙陶冶而成之，使厕足于亨途之上，某之受大造于门下也旧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1255495_comment'></div>恪居官次二年而复代归，伏遇阁下亲秉机轴，密运化钧，其所以造化生成之力，与前日不侔矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1255495_comment'></div>然而门下之士，才俊满前，得之某也未为重，失之某也不为轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1255495_comment'></div>譬犹江湖渤澥，凫雁之去来，何计于少多，则某之区区，愿曳长裾于门者，果能动阁下之听乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1255495_comment'></div>然而某闻之，古人不能为时，亦不失时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1255495_comment'></div>某之不肖，何足以知此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1255495_comment'></div>方今圣贤相逢，百废具举，苟挟一艺，莫不治其业以赴功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1255495_comment'></div>如某之愚，亦愿出寸长薄技，以无失乎斯时者，盖亦不为过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1255495_comment'></div>欂栌侏儒，有用于大厦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1255495_comment'></div>牛溲马勃，见取于名剂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1255495_comment'></div>螺甲可以助椒兰，龟壳可以齐《彖》、《象》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1255495_comment'></div>孰谓以某之贱而遽弃之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1255495_comment'></div>某之所向，而阁下不念之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1255495_comment'></div>姑诵其言而听命焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1255495_comment'></div>不宣<span class='inlineComment2'>（《云庄集》卷四。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1255495_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_106_1255495'>可：原无，据四库本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_106_1255495_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>　闲居镇江，与王彦融交游唱和。作品：《王炎弼安吉丞厅真清轩和沈文伯韵》<div id='poem_220029' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_220029' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/220029?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王炎弼安吉丞厅真清轩和沈文伯韵<span class='inlineComment2'>（炎弼名彦融，文伯名长卿）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_220029")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_220029_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_220029'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_220029'>青山如君子，臭味我族类。<div id='poem_sentence_0_220029_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_220029'>向来傲官府，正自恶俗吏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_220029_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_220029'>主人清且贤，菽水无虚伪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_220029_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_220029'>胸次尘滓尽，端可肖人意。<div id='poem_sentence_3_220029_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_220029'>轩窗自罗列，献此重叠翠。<div id='poem_sentence_4_220029_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_220029'>公馀一隐几，举目穷幽事。<div id='poem_sentence_5_220029_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_220029'>昔为幕中宾，妙语了同异。<div id='poem_sentence_6_220029_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_220029'>孰堪畏栖迟，胜境配高义。<div id='poem_sentence_7_220029_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_220029'>要从孺子濯，不逐众人醉。<div id='poem_sentence_8_220029_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_220029'>呤哦坐书丛，袖手太阿利。<div id='poem_sentence_9_220029_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_220029'>沈侯负能名，二绝一言蔽。<div id='poem_sentence_10_220029_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_220029'>聊同座右铭，此语君莫坠。<div id='poem_sentence_11_220029_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_220029'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_220029_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年9月</a>　闲居镇江，友人王彦融知楚州，代作谢表。作品：《代王楚州到任谢表》<div id='poem_1255469' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255469' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255469?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代王楚州谢到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255469")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255469_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255469'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255469'>怀章闾左，将牧远民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255469_comment'></div>下诏日边，更叨便郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255469_comment'></div>既登时而引道，乃揆日以即工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255469_comment'></div>甫见吏民，具宣德意<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255469_comment'></div>窃以国家抚广输之地，庀中外之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255469_comment'></div>任重事繁，每艰民社之寄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255469_comment'></div>地饶壤沃，莫盛江淮之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255469_comment'></div>虽中更俶扰之烦，而久遂涵濡之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255469_comment'></div>问险阻艰难之旧，恍若前生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255469_comment'></div>蒙还定安集之恩，殆将一世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255469_comment'></div>田畴日辟，户口岁增。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255469_comment'></div>信使星驰，第有劳迎之喜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255469_comment'></div>边兵雨洗，不知屯戍之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255469_comment'></div>夥矣遗黎，隐然乐国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255469_comment'></div>孰副焦劳之念，宜先慈惠之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255469_comment'></div>曾是妄庸，乃膺任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255469_comment'></div>伏念臣禀生多难，受性至愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255469_comment'></div>把玩陈编，已负传家之学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255469_comment'></div>激昂孤节，自期报上之忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255469_comment'></div>未输执耒之劳，遽遂彯缨之愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255469_comment'></div>居官白首，半为楚甸之游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255469_comment'></div>许国丹心，未断淮山之梦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255469_comment'></div>方尚须于远次，亦固守于穷途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255469_comment'></div>身留有馀，愿展肺肝之蕴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255469_comment'></div>年运而往，频惊齿发之衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255469_comment'></div>何意明纶，忽加误宠！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255469_comment'></div>此盖恭遇皇帝陛下贲明庶政，鼎养群贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255469_comment'></div>知人安民，奉天地无私之照；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255469_comment'></div>显仁藏用，合阴阳不测之神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255469_comment'></div>收精虑于九重，轸渊衷于一鄣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255469_comment'></div>肆令绵力，往布宽条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255469_comment'></div>臣敢不内竭疲驽，仰酬造化？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1255469_comment'></div>以书生而立武事，莫追家世之馀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1255469_comment'></div>帅疆吏以广诏恩，或称清时之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1255469_comment'></div>庶收微效，仰答隆私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1255469_comment'></div>八口无饥，是谓忘家之日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1255469_comment'></div>千钟不汩，但坚移孝之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1255469_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1255469_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年9月</a>　友人王彦融知楚州，作诗相送。作品：《送王炎弼赴山阳守以兵卫森画戟宴寝凝清香为韵十首》<div id='poem_219928' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_219928' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年9月11日</a>　黄祖舜拜同知枢密院事，上启致贺。作品：《贺黄同知启》<div id='poem_1255475' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255475' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255475?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺黄同知启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年9月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255475")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255475_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255475'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255475'>伏审进膺云诏，入践斗官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255475_comment'></div>庙廊居中，密运止戈之武；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255475_comment'></div>陛廉增峻，益隆助德之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255475_comment'></div>宗社奠安，官师鼓舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255475_comment'></div>窃以士得时而行道，初不知遇合之求；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255475_comment'></div>天降任于是人，必试以阨穷之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255475_comment'></div>刃历千牛而不钝，金由百鍊而愈刚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255475_comment'></div>既不失其本心，斯可临于大节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255475_comment'></div>国家总文武之柄，建丞疑之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255475_comment'></div>方当多事之时，尤重本兵之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255475_comment'></div>居帷幄之中，而知万里事机之屡至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255475_comment'></div>当尊俎之上，而识四方戍守之异宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255475_comment'></div>夫惟明足以察远微，断足以济礼变，威望足以落三军之胆，号令足以服诸将之心，独钟不世之材，斯与非常之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255475_comment'></div>恭惟某官储休星斗，钟秀山川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255475_comment'></div>洽见殚闻，专师友渊源之盛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255475_comment'></div>崇论宏议，包古今治忽之繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255475_comment'></div>既久播于英声，尝早升于华贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255475_comment'></div>穷而独善，确尔不移，时可偕行，沛然孰御？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255475_comment'></div>再履班行之旧，益推明德之隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255475_comment'></div>布心腹肾肠，擅知无不言之誉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255475_comment'></div>作股肱耳目，副人惟求旧之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255475_comment'></div>维时共政之初，翕若阿衡之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255475_comment'></div>当四郊多垒，其如责任之愈深；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255475_comment'></div>然一士可王，将见安强之有赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255475_comment'></div>某早聆盛德，辱记微踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255475_comment'></div>恩被最先，实甚泰山之仰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255475_comment'></div>身求所庇，莫如大厦之成。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1255475_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年3月</a>　赵师严（字有翼）自六院除湖州通判，有诗相送。作品：《送赵有翼通守吴兴》<div id='poem_220060' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_220060' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_220060'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_220060'>江南雨无时，桃李迹已陈。<div id='poem_sentence_0_220060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_220060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_220060'>惟公真龙种，眉宇犹津津。<div id='poem_sentence_3_220060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_220060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_220060'>去丞股肱郡，要此骨肉亲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_220060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_220060'>拄颊爱爽气，挥毫咏风蘋。<div id='poem_sentence_13_220060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_220060'>远近入题品，苍翠生精神。<div
