id='poem_sentence_16_220060'>因子动归兴，诘旦车当巾。<div id='poem_sentence_16_220060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_220060'></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_220060_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　与赵师严等唱和。作品：《赋赵有翼仇池石次沈正卿用苏翰林韵》<div id='poem_220072' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_220072' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/220072?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赋赵有翼仇池石次沈正卿用苏翰林韵<span class='inlineComment2'>（有翼名师严，正卿名清臣）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_220072")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_220072_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_220072'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_220072'>贪夫居奇货，什袭藏结绿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_220072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_220072'>宁知十五城，不救卞和足。<div id='poem_sentence_1_220072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_220072'>岂如嗜石人，丘壑在胸腹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_220072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_220072'>不知连城价，但赏数峰蹙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_220072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_220072'>长公仙去后，兵<span class='inlineComment2'>（豫章本作朔）</span>马遂南牧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_220072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_220072'>尤物落何许，心知委沟渎。<div id='poem_sentence_5_220072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_220072'>何期超世贤，爱石不爱玉。<div id='poem_sentence_6_220072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_220072'>夜半负之走，包裹随窜伏。<div id='poem_sentence_7_220072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_220072'>一朝返窗几，时清端可卜。<div id='poem_sentence_8_220072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_220072'>李虎初平羊，案上纷相逐。<div id='poem_sentence_9_220072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_220072'>峥嵘幸无恙，不问牛马谷。<div id='poem_sentence_10_220072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_220072'>赵侯天机异，阅世轻嗜欲。<div id='poem_sentence_11_220072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_220072'>好奇与嗜利，达观均一曲。<div id='poem_sentence_12_220072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_220072'>正恐便弃置，就赏君宜速。<div id='poem_sentence_13_220072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_220072'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_220072_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年10月25日</a>　张焘拜同知枢密院事，上启致贺。作品：《上张同知书》<div id='poem_1255496' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255496' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255496?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上张同知书<span class='inlineComment2'>（隆兴元年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年10月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255496")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255496_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255496'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255496'>正月十五日，承议郎、干办行在诸军粮料院曾某，谨斋沐裁书，百拜献于枢密同知阁下：某愚无似，其敢自托于先世之绪馀，言之则近于不知愧，不言则心之精微无以自见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255496_comment'></div>虽然，不敢诵言于他门而输之于门下，其亦有意矣，敢终言之，阁下试垂听焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255496_comment'></div>某世家南丰，自高、曾以降，当时先生长者，知推与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255496_comment'></div>其于推毂天下士，不翅如饥渴之于饮食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255496_comment'></div>故堙阨隐沦之贤，与夫一时之秀，往往得之而名益彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255496_comment'></div>流风遗俗，于今未泯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255496_comment'></div>某不幸，先大父捐馆舍一星终矣，而某始生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255496_comment'></div>生五年而又丧先人，甫冠而诸父无存者，其渊源所渐，益如断港绝潢也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255496_comment'></div>平时负抱手泽，慨然永叹而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255496_comment'></div>若夫自暴自弃，以为先世之辱者，虽颠倒万状，犹不忍为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255496_comment'></div>持是心以往，庶几先友之不吾弃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255496_comment'></div>又自惟念，古之人得其父祖之传，不必耳闻而目见之，盖有假之他人，而终萃于吾宗者，如鲁孔氏是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255496_comment'></div>仲尼之没，子思之年不载于传记，而伯鱼死于夫子之生存，是子思生久矣，犹未若某之声容不接也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255496_comment'></div>然子思请疑答问，不见于其先君子之书，则其弱可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255496_comment'></div>不然，以子思之资，长而立于贤父兄之侧，传道授业，当不在游、夏后，未知与颜氏之子何如耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255496_comment'></div>天将付斯文于孔氏也，曾晰为父而子舆为之子，是曾氏世有人而孔氏之所资也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255496_comment'></div>子思不得其传于父祖，而得之于子舆，是无异于传之其父子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255496_comment'></div>某之愚何敢言此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255496_comment'></div>然生世四十有四年矣，平生闻之于长老先正殿撰公，正言直道，劲气高节，挠之而不乱，涅之而不变，挽之而不回，抑之而不衰，如星日之在上，而山川之无终穷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255496_comment'></div>当是时，先大父道同志合，上下其议论，先后相汲引，而期于古人之域者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255496_comment'></div>今曾氏寖衰，而阁下德名之不替，功业之是似，关百圣、质鬼神而不可诬也，是高门之独得其传也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255496_comment'></div>夫前辈之立于世，膏馥之所沾溉，清润之所沦浃，隐然气象，望而使人之意消者，某之未见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255496_comment'></div>且某既不获亲传之父祖矣，又不能即先友之世得其传者而求之，是忘先君子于九原也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255496_comment'></div>某实惧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255496_comment'></div>恭维阁下功业塞天地，声名昭日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255496_comment'></div>高卧乡里，视富贵如浮云，而世挽留之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255496_comment'></div>夫利害交于前，而心不没于利者，古之人有能之，张子房、李长源是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255496_comment'></div>临大节，断大事，舍斯人其谁欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255496_comment'></div>此圣天子以此委之阁下，而四海之人举属望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255496_comment'></div>某于此时，始获登门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255496_comment'></div>将抽毫进牍，为短章大篇，道古今，誉盛德，以求阁下一盼之遇耶，某所不忍为而阁下之所恶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255496_comment'></div>将开口论利害，援古今，列成败，粲然如组绣之成文章，了然如烛照数计而龟卜也，某不敢先，且意阁下之不乏斯人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1255496_comment'></div>独以先友之世得其传者，惟高门为然，心悦诚服，不自知其足之及门也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1255496_comment'></div>以平昔愿见之心，相望乎千里外，始得备数司存，居德宇之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1255496_comment'></div>傥辱念其先君子之末绪，数使趋拜于左右而仰听其议论，或以为可教而幸教之，庶几失父祖之传而复于高门得之，则其为赐，宜无大于此者矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1255496_comment'></div>先君子有知，实宠绥之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1255496_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1255496_comment'></div>不知者又以为阁下持黜陟之柄，将以为阶取爵禄之资，此非某之所志，亦岂所望于门下者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1255496_comment'></div>阁下之所以赐某者，不在是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1255496_comment'></div>伏惟深察而垂纳焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1255496_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1255496_comment'></div>某皇恐百拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1255496_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　闲居镇江。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
湖州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6c12a941370a40a2a9477c06c995530b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6c12a941370a40a2a9477c06c995530b");'><span id='6c12a941370a40a2a9477c06c995530b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>，46岁</div><div id='6c12a941370a40a2a9477c06c995530b' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>寓居湖州。张孝祥除中书舍人，上启致贺。作品：《贺张舍人安国启》<div id='poem_1255480' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255480' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255480?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺张舍人安国启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255480")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255480_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255480'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255480'>窃审光对纶恩，就跻星掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255480_comment'></div>淹异材于满岁，示清朝守法之公；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255480_comment'></div>备异数于近班，彰圣世得人之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255480_comment'></div>窃以建官而训以事，自古则然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255480_comment'></div>行远而载以文，于今不废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255480_comment'></div>故书命之任，其来尚矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255480_comment'></div>而体裁之当，鲜或得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255480_comment'></div>要当无意于为文，庶几不匿于厥指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255480_comment'></div>辨忠邪而明好恶，不先偶俪之工；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255480_comment'></div>写要妙而尽精微，讵借丹青之助？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255480_comment'></div>仰惟大手，最简渊衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255480_comment'></div>播告迩遐，坦若帝王之制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255480_comment'></div>流停方册，浑然虞夏之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255480_comment'></div>果以殊知，遂加中命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255480_comment'></div>恭惟某官运逢千载，名重一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255480_comment'></div>廉折以清，琴瑟自符于均节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255480_comment'></div>温润而泽，璠玙无待于刻雕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255480_comment'></div>谠论钦议，辏于上前；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255480_comment'></div>先见明识，出于人表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255480_comment'></div>天钟大任，受圯上之一编；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255480_comment'></div>人服博闻，诵河东之三箧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255480_comment'></div>卓矣圣朝之望，翕为士论之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255480_comment'></div>自布衣结旒扆之知，古无与拟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255480_comment'></div>将端冕运甄陶之妙，今也其时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255480_comment'></div>某迹固尘埃，心驰斗岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255480_comment'></div>仰裒然之道举，识弥纶经纬之奇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255480_comment'></div>诵大哉之王言，见润色讨论之妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255480_comment'></div>共喜斯文之遂振，且知公道之方行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255480_comment'></div>顾虽疏逖之踪，同有咏歌之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255480_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1255480_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>寓居湖州。上启知湖州王师心。作品：《上湖州王尚书与道启》<div id='poem_1255482' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255482' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255482?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上湖州王尚书与道启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255482")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255482_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255482'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255482'>高门蹑履，才离竹马之群；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255482_comment'></div>乐土受廛，值奉蘋洲之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255482_comment'></div>仰德既偿于累岁，依仁复过于平生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255482_comment'></div>恭惟某官学贯九流，声高一世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255482_comment'></div>温润而泽，随所用于圭璋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255482_comment'></div>廉折以清，自成文于宫角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255482_comment'></div>卓尔万人之杰，隐然千载之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255482_comment'></div>远袭庆源，配淮水灵长之势；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255482_comment'></div>尽钟秀气，分天孙明润之辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255482_comment'></div>早追终、贾之声称，久羡严、徐之步武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255482_comment'></div>官居喉舌，实长六卿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255482_comment'></div>郡号股肱，或连千国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255482_comment'></div>轻裘缓带，屡书方面之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255482_comment'></div>閒馆珍台，聊遂燕休之适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255482_comment'></div>维名郡去长安之近，正凝旒兴宣室之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255482_comment'></div>将大属于藩条，果省图于旧德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255482_comment'></div>山川清远，暂持江海之一麾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255482_comment'></div>禁省凝严，将见承明之三入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255482_comment'></div>愿缓弓旌之贲，少勤马骑之临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255482_comment'></div>人为三公，终遂颍川之徵拜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255482_comment'></div>地方千里，且从河内之借留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255482_comment'></div>某历落亡奇，伶俜多难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255482_comment'></div>私门衰落，少尝妄意于世科；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255482_comment'></div>天分奇穷，长乃甘心于俗吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255482_comment'></div>田园索尔，丘社悠然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255482_comment'></div>巢林一枝，未遂鹪鹩之托；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255482_comment'></div>绕树三匝，方同乌鹊之惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255482_comment'></div>昨满秩于中都，偶待期于近地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255482_comment'></div>为贫而仕，作计已疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255482_comment'></div>叹异乡萍水之逢，仰仕路云泥之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255482_comment'></div>忽睹东方之骑从，乃为北道之主人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1255482_comment'></div>拭目除书，既罢草登楼之赋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1255482_comment'></div>倾心报政，或能赓乐职之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1255482_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1255482_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
吉安（吉州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7df385b94e504fffba9a0d61f7128412_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7df385b94e504fffba9a0d61f7128412");'><span id='7df385b94e504fffba9a0d61f7128412_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>，52岁</div><div id='7df385b94e504fffba9a0d61f7128412' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　是年底，知吉州。<br /></div>

-----title
抚州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='739ba8d7c2d14505996d4db55abadc44_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("739ba8d7c2d14505996d4db55abadc44");'><span id='739ba8d7c2d14505996d4db55abadc44_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>，53岁</div><div id='739ba8d7c2d14505996d4db55abadc44' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年5月</a>　五月，曾协由知吉州改知抚州。<br /></div>

-----title
零陵（永州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d2275852d54448fd8627088aed37c4a8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d2275852d54448fd8627088aed37c4a8");'><span id='d2275852d54448fd8627088aed37c4a8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1173')">1171-1173年</a>，53-55岁</div><div id='d2275852d54448fd8627088aed37c4a8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年8月</a>　八月，又由知抚州改知永州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年3月</a>　三月到任，有谢表。作品：《永州到任谢表》<div id='poem_1255467' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255467' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255467?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永州到任谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255467")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255467_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255467'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255467'>臣某言：昨准敕差权知永州军州事，臣已于三月初三日到任，望阙遥谢，交割职事管干讫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255467_comment'></div>怀组去都，久窃拜州之宠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255467_comment'></div>引麾问道，更承易地之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255467_comment'></div>始服官常，具宣德意<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255467_comment'></div>窃念臣进繇世赏，学愧家传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255467_comment'></div>少期自奋于清流，壮乃遂甘于俗吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255467_comment'></div>第谨诗书之习，粗知孝谨之传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255467_comment'></div>一践微官，寖邻膴仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255467_comment'></div>备司存于百执，参陪贰于上都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255467_comment'></div>仅逃瘝旷之愆，遽冒藩宣之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1255467_comment'></div>代为牧守，有惭万石之称；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1255467_comment'></div>官列大夫，尤乏九能之誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1255467_comment'></div>维此潇湘之会，实居楚越之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1255467_comment'></div>仍汉朝初置之名，存虞氏南巡之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1255467_comment'></div>适宽条之始布，属荒政之当修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1255467_comment'></div>虽居发粟之时，政及劝耕之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1255467_comment'></div>周原膴膴，渐施于耜之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1255467_comment'></div>陵麦青青，已兆食新之喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1255467_comment'></div>未觉居夷之陋，第惊去国之遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1255467_comment'></div>云水攀跻，敢慕宗元之纵逸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1255467_comment'></div>巅崖镵刻，愿赓元结之歌诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1255467_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下盛德曲成，至仁遍覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1255467_comment'></div>出号令九筵之邃，遵宪章三尺之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1255467_comment'></div>苦身焦心，将欲责菅茅之用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1255467_comment'></div>明目张胆，必使无瓜李之疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1255467_comment'></div>曾是微踪，荐叩改命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1255467_comment'></div>臣敢不力求民瘼，务广上恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1255467_comment'></div>分土治民，敢妄意迩遐之异；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1255467_comment'></div>因时立事，固无心宽猛之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1255467_comment'></div>庶几有补于明时，抑亦不孤于先训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1255467_comment'></div>或收薄效，仰答殊私。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1255467_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　知永州，有诗。作品：《陈晞颜董漕湖南过零陵用简斋韵见赠次韵谢之又赋一篇述怀》<div id='poem_219976' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_219976' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/219976?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈晞颜董漕湖南过零陵用简斋韵见赠次韵谢之又赋一篇述怀<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_219976")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_219976_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_219976'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_219976'>笔到钟王意有馀，诗章高古过黄初。<div id='poem_sentence_0_219976_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_219976'>班行未上论思地，远使聊宣宽大书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_219976_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_219976'>乞与丰年均饱煖，更申严令绝侵渔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_219976_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_219976'>肯迂使节存支郡，咫尺犹嫌会面疏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_219976_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_219976'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_219976_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_219975' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_219975' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/219975?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_219975_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_219975'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_219975'>平生志不在赢馀，久拟挥毫赋遂初。<div id='poem_sentence_0_219975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_219975'>莫问倚墙空甔石，但令盈几足琴书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_219975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_219975'>幸存茅屋幽堪隐，况有清溪近可渔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_219975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_219975'>剩欲抽簪访松菊，要凭突兀看扶疏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_219975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_219975'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_219975_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　知永州，有诗题郡治环翠亭。作品：《题零陵郡治环翠亭》<div id='poem_219943' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_219943' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/219943?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题零陵郡治环翠亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_219943")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_219943_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_219943'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_219943'>铃索无声讼牒稀，雨馀四野竞扶犁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_219943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_219943'>小亭独坐心无事，满地绿阴山鸟啼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_219943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_219943'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_219943_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　知永州，游淡岩有诗。作品：《和史侍郎游淡岩韵六首》<div id='poem_219902' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_219902' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/219902?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和史侍郎游澹岩韵六首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_219902")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_219902_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_219902'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_219902'>底叹兹岩省见稀，惯居故国看山围。<div id='poem_sentence_0_219902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_219902'>应缘此日慰岑寂，聊遣清诗为发挥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_219902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_219902'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_219902_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_219901' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_219901' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/219901?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_219901_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_219901'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_219901'>潇湘少驻便经年，自信孤忠莫问天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_219901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_219901'>果为冕旒勤注想，不容泉石得高眠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_219901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_219901'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_219901_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_219900' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_219900' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/219900?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_219900_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_219900'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_219900'>隐士洪崖可拍肩，尚留陈迹此山巅。<div id='poem_sentence_0_219900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_219900'>祇应千古人如在，陵谷高深却变迁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_219900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_219900'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_219900_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_219899' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_219899' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/219899?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_219899_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_219899'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_219899'>九重温诏下江边，应览甘泉旧奏篇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_219899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_219899'>却背烟岚理归棹，晓猿夜鹤总凄然。<div id='poem_sentence_1_219899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_219899'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_219899_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_219898' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_219898' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/219898?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_219898_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_219898'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_219898'>我公得入如来室，心镜常明不用磨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_219898_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_219898'>好倚悬崖结趺座，任从来者问云何。<div id='poem_sentence_1_219898_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_219898'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_219898_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_219897' class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_219897_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_219897'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_219897'>眼看岩石千寻起，面对炉烟一缕轻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_219897_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_219897'>顿觉世缘无染著，个中消息有谁明。<div id='poem_sentence_1_219897_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_219897'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_219897_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　知永州，有文《题本事方后》<div id='poem_1255507' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1255507' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1255507?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题本事方后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26720, "南宋", "曾协", "poem_title_1255507")'>曾协</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1255507_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1255507'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1255507'>某伯父谏议公绍兴丙辰岁守新安，叔舅强常州在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1255507_comment'></div>而幕中有许叔微知可，老于文学，而尤深于方书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1255507_comment'></div>伯父尝有奇疾，于是良已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1255507_comment'></div>某始闻其贤，恨未面也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1255507_comment'></div>后三十年，乃得此书于士大夫家，皆推已然之明效以告后之人，使之据旧以鉴新，言古以验今，截然易晓，不待精于医者而后能用之，又知其用心之勤且博也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1255507_comment'></div>某乾道癸巳假守零陵，因锓刻置于郡中，以广许公济众之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1255507_comment'></div>又得江夏使君历阳张之彦所记异梦，诚有补于是书，故并刻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1255507_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1255507_comment'></div>前事之不忘，后事之师也，岂独医哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1255507_comment'></div>倘能祖其所得，而遵其所戒，则何往而不利，诚可以无咎悔矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1255507_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　卒于永州任上。<br /></div>
-----end
